3926   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
3927     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
3928 
3929     array_type_mirror = null_check(array_type_mirror);
3930     original          = null_check(original);
3931 
3932     // Check if a null path was taken unconditionally.
3933     if (stopped())  return true;
3934 
3935     Node* orig_length = load_array_length(original);
3936 
3937     Node* klass_node = load_klass_from_mirror(array_type_mirror, false, NULL, 0);
3938     klass_node = null_check(klass_node);
3939 
3940     RegionNode* bailout = new RegionNode(1);
3941     record_for_igvn(bailout);
3942 
3943     // Despite the generic type of Arrays.copyOf, the mirror might be int, int[], etc.
3944     // Bail out if that is so.
3945     // Value type array may have object field that would require a
3946     // write barrier. Conservatively, go to slow path.
3947     BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
3948     Node* not_objArray = !bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(false, T_OBJECT, false, BarrierSetC2::Parsing) ?
3949         generate_typeArray_guard(klass_node, bailout) : generate_non_objArray_guard(klass_node, bailout);
3950     if (not_objArray != NULL) {
3951       // Improve the klass node's type from the new optimistic assumption:
3952       ciKlass* ak = ciArrayKlass::make(env()->Object_klass());
3953       const Type* akls = TypeKlassPtr::make(TypePtr::NotNull, ak, Type::Offset(0), false);
3954       Node* cast = new CastPPNode(klass_node, akls);
3955       cast->init_req(0, control());
3956       klass_node = _gvn.transform(cast);
3957     }
3958 
3959     Node* original_kls = load_object_klass(original);
3960     // ArrayCopyNode:Ideal may transform the ArrayCopyNode to
3961     // loads/stores but it is legal only if we're sure the
3962     // Arrays.copyOf would succeed. So we need all input arguments
3963     // to the copyOf to be validated, including that the copy to the
3964     // new array won't trigger an ArrayStoreException. That subtype
3965     // check can be optimized if we know something on the type of
3966     // the input array from type speculation.
3967     if (_gvn.type(klass_node)->singleton() && !stopped()) {
3968       ciKlass* subk   = _gvn.type(original_kls)->is_klassptr()->klass();
3969       ciKlass* superk = _gvn.type(klass_node)->is_klassptr()->klass();
3970 
3971       int test = C->static_subtype_check(superk, subk);
3972       if (test != Compile::SSC_always_true && test != Compile::SSC_always_false) {
3973         const TypeOopPtr* t_original = _gvn.type(original)->is_oopptr();
3974         if (t_original->speculative_type() != NULL) {
3975           original = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(original, t_original->speculative_type(), true);
3976           original_kls = load_object_klass(original);
3977         }
3978       }
3979     }
3980 
3981     if (ValueArrayFlatten) {
3982       // Either both or neither new array klass and original array
3983       // klass must be flattened
3984       Node* is_flat = generate_valueArray_guard(klass_node, NULL);
3985       if (!original_t->is_not_flat()) {
3986         generate_valueArray_guard(original_kls, bailout);
3987       }
3988       if (is_flat != NULL) {
3989         RegionNode* r = new RegionNode(2);
3990         record_for_igvn(r);
3991         r->init_req(1, control());
3992         set_control(is_flat);
3993         if (!original_t->is_not_flat()) {
3994           generate_valueArray_guard(original_kls, r);
3995         }
3996         bailout->add_req(control());
3997         set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
3998       }
3999     }
4000 
4001     // Bail out if either start or end is negative.
4002     generate_negative_guard(start, bailout, &start);
4003     generate_negative_guard(end,   bailout, &end);
4004 
4005     Node* length = end;
4006     if (_gvn.type(start) != TypeInt::ZERO) {
4007       length = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(end, start));
4008     }
4009 
4010     // Bail out if length is negative.
4011     // Without this the new_array would throw
4012     // NegativeArraySizeException but IllegalArgumentException is what
4013     // should be thrown
4014     generate_negative_guard(length, bailout, &length);
4015 
4016     if (bailout->req() > 1) {
4017       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4018       set_control(_gvn.transform(bailout));
4019       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
4020                     Deoptimization::Action_maybe_recompile);
4021     }
4022 
4023     if (!stopped()) {
4024       // How many elements will we copy from the original?
4025       // The answer is MinI(orig_length - start, length).
4026       Node* orig_tail = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(orig_length, start));
4027       Node* moved = generate_min_max(vmIntrinsics::_min, orig_tail, length);
4028 
4029       // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
4030       // We know the copy is disjoint but we might not know if the
4031       // oop stores need checking.
4032       // Extreme case:  Arrays.copyOf((Integer[])x, 10, String[].class).
4033       // This will fail a store-check if x contains any non-nulls.
4034 
4035       bool validated = false;
4036       // Reason_class_check rather than Reason_intrinsic because we
4037       // want to intrinsify even if this traps.
4038       if (!too_many_traps(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check)) {
4039         Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(original, klass_node);
4040 
4041         if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
4042           PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4043           set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
4044           uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_class_check,
4045                         Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
4046           assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
4047         }
4048         validated = true;
4049       }
4050 
4051       if (!stopped()) {
4052         // Load element mirror
4053         Node* p = basic_plus_adr(array_type_mirror, java_lang_Class::component_mirror_offset_in_bytes());
4054         Node* elem_mirror = access_load_at(array_type_mirror, p, _gvn.type(p)->is_ptr(), TypeInstPtr::MIRROR, T_OBJECT, IN_HEAP);
4055 
4056         newcopy = new_array(klass_node, length, 0, NULL, false, elem_mirror);
4057 
4058         ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, original, start, newcopy, intcon(0), moved, true, false,
4059                                                 original_kls, klass_node);
4060         if (!is_copyOfRange) {
4061           ac->set_copyof(validated);
4062         } else {
4063           ac->set_copyofrange(validated);
4064         }
4065         Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4066         if (n == ac) {
4067           ac->connect_outputs(this);
4068         } else {
4069           assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
4070           set_all_memory(n);
4071         }
4072       }
4073     }
4074   } // original reexecute is set back here
4075 
4076   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4077   if (!stopped()) {
4078     set_result(newcopy);
4079   }
4080   return true;
4081 }
4082 
4083 
4084 //----------------------generate_virtual_guard---------------------------
4085 // Helper for hashCode and clone.  Peeks inside the vtable to avoid a call.
4086 Node* LibraryCallKit::generate_virtual_guard(Node* obj_klass,
4087                                              RegionNode* slow_region) {
4088   ciMethod* method = callee();
4089   int vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
4090   assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
4091          "bad index %d", vtable_index);
4092   // Get the Method* out of the appropriate vtable entry.
4093   int entry_offset  = in_bytes(Klass::vtable_start_offset()) +
4094                      vtable_index*vtableEntry::size_in_bytes() +
4095                      vtableEntry::method_offset_in_bytes();
4096   Node* entry_addr  = basic_plus_adr(obj_klass, entry_offset);
4097   Node* target_call = make_load(NULL, entry_addr, TypePtr::NOTNULL, T_ADDRESS, MemNode::unordered);
4098 
4099   // Compare the target method with the expected method (e.g., Object.hashCode).
4100   const TypePtr* native_call_addr = TypeMetadataPtr::make(method);
4101 
4102   Node* native_call = makecon(native_call_addr);
4103   Node* chk_native  = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(target_call, native_call));
4104   Node* test_native = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(chk_native, BoolTest::ne));
4105 
4106   return generate_slow_guard(test_native, slow_region);
4107 }
4108 
4109 //-----------------------generate_method_call----------------------------
4110 // Use generate_method_call to make a slow-call to the real
4111 // method if the fast path fails.  An alternative would be to
4112 // use a stub like OptoRuntime::slow_arraycopy_Java.
4113 // This only works for expanding the current library call,
4114 // not another intrinsic.  (E.g., don't use this for making an
4115 // arraycopy call inside of the copyOf intrinsic.)
4116 CallJavaNode*
4117 LibraryCallKit::generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::ID method_id, bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
4118   // When compiling the intrinsic method itself, do not use this technique.
4119   guarantee(callee() != C->method(), "cannot make slow-call to self");
4120 
4121   ciMethod* method = callee();
4122   // ensure the JVMS we have will be correct for this call
4123   guarantee(method_id == method->intrinsic_id(), "must match");
4124 
4125   const TypeFunc* tf = TypeFunc::make(method);
4126   CallJavaNode* slow_call;
4127   if (is_static) {
4128     assert(!is_virtual, "");
4129     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
4130                            SharedRuntime::get_resolve_static_call_stub(),
4131                            method, bci());
4132   } else if (is_virtual) {
4133     null_check_receiver();
4134     int vtable_index = Method::invalid_vtable_index;
4135     if (UseInlineCaches) {
4136       // Suppress the vtable call
4137     } else {
4138       // hashCode and clone are not a miranda methods,
4139       // so the vtable index is fixed.
4140       // No need to use the linkResolver to get it.
4141        vtable_index = method->vtable_index();
4142        assert(vtable_index >= 0 || vtable_index == Method::nonvirtual_vtable_index,
4143               "bad index %d", vtable_index);
4144     }
4145     slow_call = new CallDynamicJavaNode(tf,
4146                           SharedRuntime::get_resolve_virtual_call_stub(),
4147                           method, vtable_index, bci());
4148   } else {  // neither virtual nor static:  opt_virtual
4149     null_check_receiver();
4150     slow_call = new CallStaticJavaNode(C, tf,
4151                                 SharedRuntime::get_resolve_opt_virtual_call_stub(),
4152                                 method, bci());
4153     slow_call->set_optimized_virtual(true);
4154   }
4155   if (CallGenerator::is_inlined_method_handle_intrinsic(this->method(), bci(), callee())) {
4156     // To be able to issue a direct call (optimized virtual or virtual)
4157     // and skip a call to MH.linkTo*/invokeBasic adapter, additional information
4158     // about the method being invoked should be attached to the call site to
4159     // make resolution logic work (see SharedRuntime::resolve_{virtual,opt_virtual}_call_C).
4160     slow_call->set_override_symbolic_info(true);
4161   }
4162   set_arguments_for_java_call(slow_call);
4163   set_edges_for_java_call(slow_call);
4164   return slow_call;
4165 }
4166 
4167 
4168 /**
4169  * Build special case code for calls to hashCode on an object. This call may
4170  * be virtual (invokevirtual) or bound (invokespecial). For each case we generate
4171  * slightly different code.
4172  */
4173 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_hashcode(bool is_virtual, bool is_static) {
4174   assert(is_static == callee()->is_static(), "correct intrinsic selection");
4175   assert(!(is_virtual && is_static), "either virtual, special, or static");
4176 
4177   enum { _slow_path = 1, _fast_path, _null_path, PATH_LIMIT };
4178 
4179   RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
4180   PhiNode*    result_val = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInt::INT);
4181   PhiNode*    result_io  = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
4182   PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
4183   Node* obj = argument(0);
4184 
4185   if (obj->is_ValueType() || gvn().type(obj)->is_valuetypeptr()) {
4186     return false;
4187   }
4188 
4189   if (!is_static) {
4190     // Check for hashing null object
4191     obj = null_check_receiver();
4192     if (stopped())  return true;        // unconditionally null
4193     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, top());
4194     result_val->init_req(_null_path, top());
4195   } else {
4196     // Do a null check, and return zero if null.
4197     // System.identityHashCode(null) == 0
4198     Node* null_ctl = top();
4199     obj = null_check_oop(obj, &null_ctl);
4200     result_reg->init_req(_null_path, null_ctl);
4201     result_val->init_req(_null_path, _gvn.intcon(0));
4202   }
4203 
4204   // Unconditionally null?  Then return right away.
4205   if (stopped()) {
4206     set_control( result_reg->in(_null_path));
4207     if (!stopped())
4208       set_result(result_val->in(_null_path));
4209     return true;
4210   }
4211 
4212   // We only go to the fast case code if we pass a number of guards.  The
4213   // paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
4214   RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4215   record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4216 
4217   // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We pull out
4218   // the vtable entry corresponding to hashCode() from the target object.
4219   // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the native
4220   // Object hashCode() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
4221   // guard for non-virtual calls -- the caller is known to be the native
4222   // Object hashCode().
4223   if (is_virtual) {
4224     // After null check, get the object's klass.
4225     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
4226     generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4227   }
4228 
4229   // Get the header out of the object, use LoadMarkNode when available
4230   Node* header_addr = basic_plus_adr(obj, oopDesc::mark_offset_in_bytes());
4231   // The control of the load must be NULL. Otherwise, the load can move before
4232   // the null check after castPP removal.
4233   Node* no_ctrl = NULL;
4234   Node* header = make_load(no_ctrl, header_addr, TypeX_X, TypeX_X->basic_type(), MemNode::unordered);
4235 
4236   // Test the header to see if it is unlocked.
4237   // This also serves as guard against value types (they have the always_locked_pattern set).
4238   Node *lock_mask      = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::biased_lock_mask_in_place);
4239   Node *lmasked_header = _gvn.transform(new AndXNode(header, lock_mask));
4240   Node *unlocked_val   = _gvn.MakeConX(markWord::unlocked_value);
4241   Node *chk_unlocked   = _gvn.transform(new CmpXNode( lmasked_header, unlocked_val));
4242   Node *test_unlocked  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_unlocked, BoolTest::ne));
4243 
4244   generate_slow_guard(test_unlocked, slow_region);
4245 
4246   // Get the hash value and check to see that it has been properly assigned.
4247   // We depend on hash_mask being at most 32 bits and avoid the use of
4248   // hash_mask_in_place because it could be larger than 32 bits in a 64-bit
4249   // vm: see markWord.hpp.
4250   Node *hash_mask      = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_mask);
4251   Node *hash_shift     = _gvn.intcon(markWord::hash_shift);
4252   Node *hshifted_header= _gvn.transform(new URShiftXNode(header, hash_shift));
4253   // This hack lets the hash bits live anywhere in the mark object now, as long
4254   // as the shift drops the relevant bits into the low 32 bits.  Note that
4255   // Java spec says that HashCode is an int so there's no point in capturing
4256   // an 'X'-sized hashcode (32 in 32-bit build or 64 in 64-bit build).
4257   hshifted_header      = ConvX2I(hshifted_header);
4258   Node *hash_val       = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(hshifted_header, hash_mask));
4259 
4260   Node *no_hash_val    = _gvn.intcon(markWord::no_hash);
4261   Node *chk_assigned   = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode( hash_val, no_hash_val));
4262   Node *test_assigned  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode( chk_assigned, BoolTest::eq));
4263 
4264   generate_slow_guard(test_assigned, slow_region);
4265 
4266   Node* init_mem = reset_memory();
4267   // fill in the rest of the null path:
4268   result_io ->init_req(_null_path, i_o());
4269   result_mem->init_req(_null_path, init_mem);
4270 
4271   result_val->init_req(_fast_path, hash_val);
4272   result_reg->init_req(_fast_path, control());
4273   result_io ->init_req(_fast_path, i_o());
4274   result_mem->init_req(_fast_path, init_mem);
4275 
4276   // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to hashCode().
4277   set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4278   if (!stopped()) {
4279     // No need for PreserveJVMState, because we're using up the present state.
4280     set_all_memory(init_mem);
4281     vmIntrinsics::ID hashCode_id = is_static ? vmIntrinsics::_identityHashCode : vmIntrinsics::_hashCode;
4282     CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(hashCode_id, is_virtual, is_static);
4283     Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call);
4284     // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
4285     result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
4286     result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
4287     result_io  ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
4288     result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
4289   }
4290 
4291   // Return the combined state.
4292   set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_io)  );
4293   set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
4294 
4295   set_result(result_reg, result_val);
4296   return true;
4297 }
4298 
4299 //---------------------------inline_native_getClass----------------------------
4300 // public final native Class<?> java.lang.Object.getClass();
4301 //
4302 // Build special case code for calls to getClass on an object.
4303 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_getClass() {
4304   Node* obj = argument(0);
4305   if (obj->is_ValueType()) {
4306     ciKlass* vk = _gvn.type(obj)->value_klass();
4307     set_result(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(vk->java_mirror())));
4308     return true;
4309   }
4310   obj = null_check_receiver();
4311   if (stopped())  return true;
4312   set_result(load_mirror_from_klass(load_object_klass(obj)));
4313   return true;
4314 }
4315 
4316 //-----------------inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass---------------------
4317 // public static native Class<?> sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass();
4318 //
4319 // In the presence of deep enough inlining, getCallerClass() becomes a no-op.
4320 //
4321 // NOTE: This code must perform the same logic as JVM_GetCallerClass
4322 // in that it must skip particular security frames and checks for
4323 // caller sensitive methods.
4324 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_Reflection_getCallerClass() {
4325 #ifndef PRODUCT
4326   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4327     tty->print_cr("Attempting to inline sun.reflect.Reflection.getCallerClass");
4328   }
4329 #endif
4330 
4331   if (!jvms()->has_method()) {
4332 #ifndef PRODUCT
4333     if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4334       tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because intrinsic was inlined at top level");
4335     }
4336 #endif
4337     return false;
4338   }
4339 
4340   // Walk back up the JVM state to find the caller at the required
4341   // depth.
4342   JVMState* caller_jvms = jvms();
4343 
4344   // Cf. JVM_GetCallerClass
4345   // NOTE: Start the loop at depth 1 because the current JVM state does
4346   // not include the Reflection.getCallerClass() frame.
4347   for (int n = 1; caller_jvms != NULL; caller_jvms = caller_jvms->caller(), n++) {
4348     ciMethod* m = caller_jvms->method();
4349     switch (n) {
4350     case 0:
4351       fatal("current JVM state does not include the Reflection.getCallerClass frame");
4352       break;
4353     case 1:
4354       // Frame 0 and 1 must be caller sensitive (see JVM_GetCallerClass).
4355       if (!m->caller_sensitive()) {
4356 #ifndef PRODUCT
4357         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4358           tty->print_cr("  Bailing out: CallerSensitive annotation expected at frame %d", n);
4359         }
4360 #endif
4361         return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4362       }
4363       break;
4364     default:
4365       if (!m->is_ignored_by_security_stack_walk()) {
4366         // We have reached the desired frame; return the holder class.
4367         // Acquire method holder as java.lang.Class and push as constant.
4368         ciInstanceKlass* caller_klass = caller_jvms->method()->holder();
4369         ciInstance* caller_mirror = caller_klass->java_mirror();
4370         set_result(makecon(TypeInstPtr::make(caller_mirror)));
4371 
4372 #ifndef PRODUCT
4373         if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4374           tty->print_cr("  Succeeded: caller = %d) %s.%s, JVMS depth = %d", n, caller_klass->name()->as_utf8(), caller_jvms->method()->name()->as_utf8(), jvms()->depth());
4375           tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4376           for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4377             ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4378             tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4379           }
4380         }
4381 #endif
4382         return true;
4383       }
4384       break;
4385     }
4386   }
4387 
4388 #ifndef PRODUCT
4389   if ((C->print_intrinsics() || C->print_inlining()) && Verbose) {
4390     tty->print_cr("  Bailing out because caller depth exceeded inlining depth = %d", jvms()->depth());
4391     tty->print_cr("  JVM state at this point:");
4392     for (int i = jvms()->depth(), n = 1; i >= 1; i--, n++) {
4393       ciMethod* m = jvms()->of_depth(i)->method();
4394       tty->print_cr("   %d) %s.%s", n, m->holder()->name()->as_utf8(), m->name()->as_utf8());
4395     }
4396   }
4397 #endif
4398 
4399   return false;  // bail-out; let JVM_GetCallerClass do the work
4400 }
4401 
4402 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_conversions(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
4403   Node* arg = argument(0);
4404   Node* result = NULL;
4405 
4406   switch (id) {
4407   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToRawIntBits:    result = new MoveF2INode(arg);  break;
4408   case vmIntrinsics::_intBitsToFloat:       result = new MoveI2FNode(arg);  break;
4409   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToRawLongBits:  result = new MoveD2LNode(arg);  break;
4410   case vmIntrinsics::_longBitsToDouble:     result = new MoveL2DNode(arg);  break;
4411 
4412   case vmIntrinsics::_doubleToLongBits: {
4413     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4414     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4415     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeLong::LONG);
4416 
4417     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpDNode(arg, arg));
4418     // Build the boolean node
4419     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4420 
4421     // Branch either way.
4422     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4423     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4424     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4425     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4426     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4427     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4428 
4429     set_control(iftrue);
4430 
4431     static const jlong nan_bits = CONST64(0x7ff8000000000000);
4432     Node *slow_result = longcon(nan_bits); // return NaN
4433     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4434     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4435 
4436     // Else fall through
4437     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4438     set_control(iffalse);
4439 
4440     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveD2LNode(arg)));
4441     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4442 
4443     // Post merge
4444     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4445     record_for_igvn(r);
4446 
4447     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4448     result = phi;
4449     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_long(), "must be");
4450     break;
4451   }
4452 
4453   case vmIntrinsics::_floatToIntBits: {
4454     // two paths (plus control) merge in a wood
4455     RegionNode *r = new RegionNode(3);
4456     Node *phi = new PhiNode(r, TypeInt::INT);
4457 
4458     Node *cmpisnan = _gvn.transform(new CmpFNode(arg, arg));
4459     // Build the boolean node
4460     Node *bolisnan = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmpisnan, BoolTest::ne));
4461 
4462     // Branch either way.
4463     // NaN case is less traveled, which makes all the difference.
4464     IfNode *ifisnan = create_and_xform_if(control(), bolisnan, PROB_STATIC_FREQUENT, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
4465     Node *opt_isnan = _gvn.transform(ifisnan);
4466     assert( opt_isnan->is_If(), "Expect an IfNode");
4467     IfNode *opt_ifisnan = (IfNode*)opt_isnan;
4468     Node *iftrue = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(opt_ifisnan));
4469 
4470     set_control(iftrue);
4471 
4472     static const jint nan_bits = 0x7fc00000;
4473     Node *slow_result = makecon(TypeInt::make(nan_bits)); // return NaN
4474     phi->init_req(1, _gvn.transform( slow_result ));
4475     r->init_req(1, iftrue);
4476 
4477     // Else fall through
4478     Node *iffalse = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(opt_ifisnan));
4479     set_control(iffalse);
4480 
4481     phi->init_req(2, _gvn.transform(new MoveF2INode(arg)));
4482     r->init_req(2, iffalse);
4483 
4484     // Post merge
4485     set_control(_gvn.transform(r));
4486     record_for_igvn(r);
4487 
4488     C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
4489     result = phi;
4490     assert(result->bottom_type()->isa_int(), "must be");
4491     break;
4492   }
4493 
4494   default:
4495     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
4496     break;
4497   }
4498   set_result(_gvn.transform(result));
4499   return true;
4500 }
4501 
4502 //----------------------inline_unsafe_copyMemory-------------------------
4503 // public native void Unsafe.copyMemory0(Object srcBase, long srcOffset, Object destBase, long destOffset, long bytes);
4504 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_unsafe_copyMemory() {
4505   if (callee()->is_static())  return false;  // caller must have the capability!
4506   null_check_receiver();  // null-check receiver
4507   if (stopped())  return true;
4508 
4509   C->set_has_unsafe_access(true);  // Mark eventual nmethod as "unsafe".
4510 
4511   Node* src_ptr =         argument(1);   // type: oop
4512   Node* src_off = ConvL2X(argument(2));  // type: long
4513   Node* dst_ptr =         argument(4);   // type: oop
4514   Node* dst_off = ConvL2X(argument(5));  // type: long
4515   Node* size    = ConvL2X(argument(7));  // type: long
4516 
4517   assert(Unsafe_field_offset_to_byte_offset(11) == 11,
4518          "fieldOffset must be byte-scaled");
4519 
4520   Node* src = make_unsafe_address(src_ptr, src_off, ACCESS_READ);
4521   Node* dst = make_unsafe_address(dst_ptr, dst_off, ACCESS_WRITE);
4522 
4523   // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4524   // Do not let writes of the copy source or destination float below the copy.
4525   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4526 
4527   Node* thread = _gvn.transform(new ThreadLocalNode());
4528   Node* doing_unsafe_access_addr = basic_plus_adr(top(), thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::doing_unsafe_access_offset()));
4529   BasicType doing_unsafe_access_bt = T_BYTE;
4530   assert((sizeof(bool) * CHAR_BIT) == 8, "not implemented");
4531 
4532   // update volatile field
4533   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(1), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4534 
4535   // Call it.  Note that the length argument is not scaled.
4536   make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
4537                     OptoRuntime::fast_arraycopy_Type(),
4538                     StubRoutines::unsafe_arraycopy(),
4539                     "unsafe_arraycopy",
4540                     TypeRawPtr::BOTTOM,
4541                     src, dst, size XTOP);
4542 
4543   store_to_memory(control(), doing_unsafe_access_addr, intcon(0), doing_unsafe_access_bt, Compile::AliasIdxRaw, MemNode::unordered);
4544 
4545   // Do not let reads of the copy destination float above the copy.
4546   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4547 
4548   return true;
4549 }
4550 
4551 //------------------------clone_coping-----------------------------------
4552 // Helper function for inline_native_clone.
4553 void LibraryCallKit::copy_to_clone(Node* obj, Node* alloc_obj, Node* obj_size, bool is_array) {
4554   assert(obj_size != NULL, "");
4555   Node* raw_obj = alloc_obj->in(1);
4556   assert(alloc_obj->is_CheckCastPP() && raw_obj->is_Proj() && raw_obj->in(0)->is_Allocate(), "");
4557 
4558   AllocateNode* alloc = NULL;
4559   if (ReduceBulkZeroing) {
4560     // We will be completely responsible for initializing this object -
4561     // mark Initialize node as complete.
4562     alloc = AllocateNode::Ideal_allocation(alloc_obj, &_gvn);
4563     // The object was just allocated - there should be no any stores!
4564     guarantee(alloc != NULL && alloc->maybe_set_complete(&_gvn), "");
4565     // Mark as complete_with_arraycopy so that on AllocateNode
4566     // expansion, we know this AllocateNode is initialized by an array
4567     // copy and a StoreStore barrier exists after the array copy.
4568     alloc->initialization()->set_complete_with_arraycopy();
4569   }
4570 
4571   Node* size = _gvn.transform(obj_size);
4572   // Exclude the header but include array length to copy by 8 bytes words.
4573   // Can't use base_offset_in_bytes(bt) since basic type is unknown.
4574   int base_off = BarrierSetC2::arraycopy_payload_base_offset(is_array);
4575   Node* src_base  = basic_plus_adr(obj,  base_off);
4576   Node* dst_base = basic_plus_adr(alloc_obj, base_off);
4577 
4578   // Compute the length also, if needed:
4579   Node* countx = size;
4580   countx = _gvn.transform(new SubXNode(countx, MakeConX(base_off)));
4581   countx = _gvn.transform(new URShiftXNode(countx, intcon(LogBytesPerLong)));
4582 
4583   access_clone(src_base, dst_base, countx, is_array);
4584 
4585   // Do not let reads from the cloned object float above the arraycopy.
4586   if (alloc != NULL) {
4587     // Do not let stores that initialize this object be reordered with
4588     // a subsequent store that would make this object accessible by
4589     // other threads.
4590     // Record what AllocateNode this StoreStore protects so that
4591     // escape analysis can go from the MemBarStoreStoreNode to the
4592     // AllocateNode and eliminate the MemBarStoreStoreNode if possible
4593     // based on the escape status of the AllocateNode.
4594     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarStoreStore, alloc->proj_out_or_null(AllocateNode::RawAddress));
4595   } else {
4596     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4597   }
4598 }
4599 
4600 //------------------------inline_native_clone----------------------------
4601 // protected native Object java.lang.Object.clone();
4602 //
4603 // Here are the simple edge cases:
4604 //  null receiver => normal trap
4605 //  virtual and clone was overridden => slow path to out-of-line clone
4606 //  not cloneable or finalizer => slow path to out-of-line Object.clone
4607 //
4608 // The general case has two steps, allocation and copying.
4609 // Allocation has two cases, and uses GraphKit::new_instance or new_array.
4610 //
4611 // Copying also has two cases, oop arrays and everything else.
4612 // Oop arrays use arrayof_oop_arraycopy (same as System.arraycopy).
4613 // Everything else uses the tight inline loop supplied by CopyArrayNode.
4614 //
4615 // These steps fold up nicely if and when the cloned object's klass
4616 // can be sharply typed as an object array, a type array, or an instance.
4617 //
4618 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_native_clone(bool is_virtual) {
4619   PhiNode* result_val;
4620 
4621   // Set the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
4622   // the bytecode that invokes Object.clone if deoptimization happens.
4623   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
4624     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
4625 
4626     Node* obj = argument(0);
4627     if (obj->is_ValueType()) {
4628       return false;
4629     }
4630 
4631     obj = null_check_receiver();
4632     if (stopped())  return true;
4633 
4634     const TypeOopPtr* obj_type = _gvn.type(obj)->is_oopptr();
4635 
4636     // If we are going to clone an instance, we need its exact type to
4637     // know the number and types of fields to convert the clone to
4638     // loads/stores. Maybe a speculative type can help us.
4639     if (!obj_type->klass_is_exact() &&
4640         obj_type->speculative_type() != NULL &&
4641         obj_type->speculative_type()->is_instance_klass() &&
4642         !obj_type->speculative_type()->is_valuetype()) {
4643       ciInstanceKlass* spec_ik = obj_type->speculative_type()->as_instance_klass();
4644       if (spec_ik->nof_nonstatic_fields() <= ArrayCopyLoadStoreMaxElem &&
4645           !spec_ik->has_injected_fields()) {
4646         ciKlass* k = obj_type->klass();
4647         if (!k->is_instance_klass() ||
4648             k->as_instance_klass()->is_interface() ||
4649             k->as_instance_klass()->has_subklass()) {
4650           obj = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(obj, obj_type->speculative_type(), false);
4651         }
4652       }
4653     }
4654 
4655     // Conservatively insert a memory barrier on all memory slices.
4656     // Do not let writes into the original float below the clone.
4657     insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
4658 
4659     // paths into result_reg:
4660     enum {
4661       _slow_path = 1,     // out-of-line call to clone method (virtual or not)
4662       _objArray_path,     // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_oop_arraycopy
4663       _array_path,        // plain array allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4664       _instance_path,     // plain instance allocation, plus arrayof_long_arraycopy
4665       PATH_LIMIT
4666     };
4667     RegionNode* result_reg = new RegionNode(PATH_LIMIT);
4668     result_val             = new PhiNode(result_reg, TypeInstPtr::NOTNULL);
4669     PhiNode*    result_i_o = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::ABIO);
4670     PhiNode*    result_mem = new PhiNode(result_reg, Type::MEMORY, TypePtr::BOTTOM);
4671     record_for_igvn(result_reg);
4672 
4673     Node* obj_klass = load_object_klass(obj);
4674     // We only go to the fast case code if we pass a number of guards.
4675     // The paths which do not pass are accumulated in the slow_region.
4676     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
4677     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
4678 
4679     Node* array_ctl = generate_array_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4680     if (array_ctl != NULL) {
4681       // It's an array.
4682       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4683       set_control(array_ctl);
4684 
4685       BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
4686       if (bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(true, T_OBJECT, true, BarrierSetC2::Parsing) &&
4687           (!obj_type->isa_aryptr() || !obj_type->is_aryptr()->is_not_flat())) {
4688         // Flattened value type array may have object field that would require a
4689         // write barrier. Conservatively, go to slow path.
4690         generate_valueArray_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4691       }
4692 
4693       if (!stopped()) {
4694         Node* obj_length = load_array_length(obj);
4695         Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4696         // Load element mirror
4697         Node* array_type_mirror = load_mirror_from_klass(obj_klass);
4698         Node* p = basic_plus_adr(array_type_mirror, java_lang_Class::component_mirror_offset_in_bytes());
4699         Node* elem_mirror = access_load_at(array_type_mirror, p, _gvn.type(p)->is_ptr(), TypeInstPtr::MIRROR, T_OBJECT, IN_HEAP);
4700 
4701         Node* alloc_obj = new_array(obj_klass, obj_length, 0, &obj_size, false, elem_mirror);
4702 
4703         BarrierSetC2* bs = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_c2();
4704         if (bs->array_copy_requires_gc_barriers(true, T_OBJECT, true, BarrierSetC2::Parsing)) {
4705           // If it is an oop array, it requires very special treatment,
4706           // because gc barriers are required when accessing the array.
4707           Node* is_obja = generate_objArray_guard(obj_klass, (RegionNode*)NULL);
4708           if (is_obja != NULL) {
4709             PreserveJVMState pjvms2(this);
4710             set_control(is_obja);
4711             // Generate a direct call to the right arraycopy function(s).
4712             Node* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(alloc_obj, NULL);
4713             ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, obj, intcon(0), alloc_obj, intcon(0), obj_length, alloc != NULL, false);
4714             ac->set_clone_oop_array();
4715             Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
4716             assert(n == ac, "cannot disappear");
4717             ac->connect_outputs(this);
4718 
4719             result_reg->init_req(_objArray_path, control());
4720             result_val->init_req(_objArray_path, alloc_obj);
4721             result_i_o ->set_req(_objArray_path, i_o());
4722             result_mem ->set_req(_objArray_path, reset_memory());
4723           }
4724         }
4725         // Otherwise, there are no barriers to worry about.
4726         // (We can dispense with card marks if we know the allocation
4727         //  comes out of eden (TLAB)...  In fact, ReduceInitialCardMarks
4728         //  causes the non-eden paths to take compensating steps to
4729         //  simulate a fresh allocation, so that no further
4730         //  card marks are required in compiled code to initialize
4731         //  the object.)
4732 
4733         if (!stopped()) {
4734           copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, true);
4735 
4736           // Present the results of the copy.
4737           result_reg->init_req(_array_path, control());
4738           result_val->init_req(_array_path, alloc_obj);
4739           result_i_o ->set_req(_array_path, i_o());
4740           result_mem ->set_req(_array_path, reset_memory());
4741         }
4742       }
4743     }
4744 
4745     if (!stopped()) {
4746       // It's an instance (we did array above).  Make the slow-path tests.
4747       // If this is a virtual call, we generate a funny guard.  We grab
4748       // the vtable entry corresponding to clone() from the target object.
4749       // If the target method which we are calling happens to be the
4750       // Object clone() method, we pass the guard.  We do not need this
4751       // guard for non-virtual calls; the caller is known to be the native
4752       // Object clone().
4753       if (is_virtual) {
4754         generate_virtual_guard(obj_klass, slow_region);
4755       }
4756 
4757       // The object must be easily cloneable and must not have a finalizer.
4758       // Both of these conditions may be checked in a single test.
4759       // We could optimize the test further, but we don't care.
4760       generate_access_flags_guard(obj_klass,
4761                                   // Test both conditions:
4762                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST | JVM_ACC_HAS_FINALIZER,
4763                                   // Must be cloneable but not finalizer:
4764                                   JVM_ACC_IS_CLONEABLE_FAST,
4765                                   slow_region);
4766     }
4767 
4768     if (!stopped()) {
4769       // It's an instance, and it passed the slow-path tests.
4770       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4771       Node* obj_size  = NULL;
4772       // Need to deoptimize on exception from allocation since Object.clone intrinsic
4773       // is reexecuted if deoptimization occurs and there could be problems when merging
4774       // exception state between multiple Object.clone versions (reexecute=true vs reexecute=false).
4775       Node* alloc_obj = new_instance(obj_klass, NULL, &obj_size, /*deoptimize_on_exception=*/true);
4776 
4777       copy_to_clone(obj, alloc_obj, obj_size, false);
4778 
4779       // Present the results of the slow call.
4780       result_reg->init_req(_instance_path, control());
4781       result_val->init_req(_instance_path, alloc_obj);
4782       result_i_o ->set_req(_instance_path, i_o());
4783       result_mem ->set_req(_instance_path, reset_memory());
4784     }
4785 
4786     // Generate code for the slow case.  We make a call to clone().
4787     set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
4788     if (!stopped()) {
4789       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
4790       CallJavaNode* slow_call = generate_method_call(vmIntrinsics::_clone, is_virtual);
4791       // We need to deoptimize on exception (see comment above)
4792       Node* slow_result = set_results_for_java_call(slow_call, false, /* deoptimize */ true);
4793       // this->control() comes from set_results_for_java_call
4794       result_reg->init_req(_slow_path, control());
4795       result_val->init_req(_slow_path, slow_result);
4796       result_i_o ->set_req(_slow_path, i_o());
4797       result_mem ->set_req(_slow_path, reset_memory());
4798     }
4799 
4800     // Return the combined state.
4801     set_control(    _gvn.transform(result_reg));
4802     set_i_o(        _gvn.transform(result_i_o));
4803     set_all_memory( _gvn.transform(result_mem));
4804   } // original reexecute is set back here
4805 
4806   set_result(_gvn.transform(result_val));
4807   return true;
4808 }
4809 
4810 // If we have a tightly coupled allocation, the arraycopy may take care
4811 // of the array initialization. If one of the guards we insert between
4812 // the allocation and the arraycopy causes a deoptimization, an
4813 // unitialized array will escape the compiled method. To prevent that
4814 // we set the JVM state for uncommon traps between the allocation and
4815 // the arraycopy to the state before the allocation so, in case of
4816 // deoptimization, we'll reexecute the allocation and the
4817 // initialization.
4818 JVMState* LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, int& saved_reexecute_sp) {
4819   if (alloc != NULL) {
4820     ciMethod* trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
4821     int trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
4822 
4823     if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
4824         !C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_null_check)) {
4825       // Make sure there's no store between the allocation and the
4826       // arraycopy otherwise visible side effects could be rexecuted
4827       // in case of deoptimization and cause incorrect execution.
4828       bool no_interfering_store = true;
4829       Node* mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4830       if (mem->is_MergeMem()) {
4831         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory(), mem->as_MergeMem()); mms.next_non_empty2(); ) {
4832           Node* n = mms.memory();
4833           if (n != mms.memory2() && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4834             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4835             no_interfering_store = false;
4836             break;
4837           }
4838         }
4839       } else {
4840         for (MergeMemStream mms(merged_memory()); mms.next_non_empty(); ) {
4841           Node* n = mms.memory();
4842           if (n != mem && !(n->is_Proj() && n->in(0) == alloc->initialization())) {
4843             assert(n->is_Store(), "what else?");
4844             no_interfering_store = false;
4845             break;
4846           }
4847         }
4848       }
4849 
4850       if (no_interfering_store) {
4851         JVMState* old_jvms = alloc->jvms()->clone_shallow(C);
4852         uint size = alloc->req();
4853         SafePointNode* sfpt = new SafePointNode(size, old_jvms);
4854         old_jvms->set_map(sfpt);
4855         for (uint i = 0; i < size; i++) {
4856           sfpt->init_req(i, alloc->in(i));
4857         }
4858         // re-push array length for deoptimization
4859         sfpt->ins_req(old_jvms->stkoff() + old_jvms->sp(), alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4860         old_jvms->set_sp(old_jvms->sp()+1);
4861         old_jvms->set_monoff(old_jvms->monoff()+1);
4862         old_jvms->set_scloff(old_jvms->scloff()+1);
4863         old_jvms->set_endoff(old_jvms->endoff()+1);
4864         old_jvms->set_should_reexecute(true);
4865 
4866         sfpt->set_i_o(map()->i_o());
4867         sfpt->set_memory(map()->memory());
4868         sfpt->set_control(map()->control());
4869 
4870         JVMState* saved_jvms = jvms();
4871         saved_reexecute_sp = _reexecute_sp;
4872 
4873         set_jvms(sfpt->jvms());
4874         _reexecute_sp = jvms()->sp();
4875 
4876         return saved_jvms;
4877       }
4878     }
4879   }
4880   return NULL;
4881 }
4882 
4883 // In case of a deoptimization, we restart execution at the
4884 // allocation, allocating a new array. We would leave an uninitialized
4885 // array in the heap that GCs wouldn't expect. Move the allocation
4886 // after the traps so we don't allocate the array if we
4887 // deoptimize. This is possible because tightly_coupled_allocation()
4888 // guarantees there's no observer of the allocated array at this point
4889 // and the control flow is simple enough.
4890 void LibraryCallKit::arraycopy_move_allocation_here(AllocateArrayNode* alloc, Node* dest, JVMState* saved_jvms,
4891                                                     int saved_reexecute_sp, uint new_idx) {
4892   if (saved_jvms != NULL && !stopped()) {
4893     assert(alloc != NULL, "only with a tightly coupled allocation");
4894     // restore JVM state to the state at the arraycopy
4895     saved_jvms->map()->set_control(map()->control());
4896     assert(saved_jvms->map()->memory() == map()->memory(), "memory state changed?");
4897     assert(saved_jvms->map()->i_o() == map()->i_o(), "IO state changed?");
4898     // If we've improved the types of some nodes (null check) while
4899     // emitting the guards, propagate them to the current state
4900     map()->replaced_nodes().apply(saved_jvms->map(), new_idx);
4901     set_jvms(saved_jvms);
4902     _reexecute_sp = saved_reexecute_sp;
4903 
4904     // Remove the allocation from above the guards
4905     CallProjections* callprojs = alloc->extract_projections(true);
4906     InitializeNode* init = alloc->initialization();
4907     Node* alloc_mem = alloc->in(TypeFunc::Memory);
4908     C->gvn_replace_by(callprojs->fallthrough_ioproj, alloc->in(TypeFunc::I_O));
4909     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Memory), alloc_mem);
4910     C->gvn_replace_by(init->proj_out(TypeFunc::Control), alloc->in(0));
4911 
4912     // move the allocation here (after the guards)
4913     _gvn.hash_delete(alloc);
4914     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Control, control());
4915     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::I_O, i_o());
4916     Node *mem = reset_memory();
4917     set_all_memory(mem);
4918     alloc->set_req(TypeFunc::Memory, mem);
4919     set_control(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Control));
4920     set_i_o(callprojs->fallthrough_ioproj);
4921 
4922     // Update memory as done in GraphKit::set_output_for_allocation()
4923     const TypeInt* length_type = _gvn.find_int_type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::ALength));
4924     const TypeOopPtr* ary_type = _gvn.type(alloc->in(AllocateNode::KlassNode))->is_klassptr()->as_instance_type();
4925     if (ary_type->isa_aryptr() && length_type != NULL) {
4926       ary_type = ary_type->is_aryptr()->cast_to_size(length_type);
4927     }
4928     const TypePtr* telemref = ary_type->add_offset(Type::OffsetBot);
4929     int            elemidx  = C->get_alias_index(telemref);
4930     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
4931     set_memory(init->proj_out_or_null(TypeFunc::Memory), elemidx);
4932 
4933     Node* allocx = _gvn.transform(alloc);
4934     assert(allocx == alloc, "where has the allocation gone?");
4935     assert(dest->is_CheckCastPP(), "not an allocation result?");
4936 
4937     _gvn.hash_delete(dest);
4938     dest->set_req(0, control());
4939     Node* destx = _gvn.transform(dest);
4940     assert(destx == dest, "where has the allocation result gone?");
4941   }
4942 }
4943 
4944 
4945 //------------------------------inline_arraycopy-----------------------
4946 // public static native void java.lang.System.arraycopy(Object src,  int  srcPos,
4947 //                                                      Object dest, int destPos,
4948 //                                                      int length);
4949 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_arraycopy() {
4950   // Get the arguments.
4951   Node* src         = argument(0);  // type: oop
4952   Node* src_offset  = argument(1);  // type: int
4953   Node* dest        = argument(2);  // type: oop
4954   Node* dest_offset = argument(3);  // type: int
4955   Node* length      = argument(4);  // type: int
4956 
4957   uint new_idx = C->unique();
4958 
4959   // Check for allocation before we add nodes that would confuse
4960   // tightly_coupled_allocation()
4961   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4962 
4963   int saved_reexecute_sp = -1;
4964   JVMState* saved_jvms = arraycopy_restore_alloc_state(alloc, saved_reexecute_sp);
4965   // See arraycopy_restore_alloc_state() comment
4966   // if alloc == NULL we don't have to worry about a tightly coupled allocation so we can emit all needed guards
4967   // if saved_jvms != NULL (then alloc != NULL) then we can handle guards and a tightly coupled allocation
4968   // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we can't emit any guards
4969   bool can_emit_guards = (alloc == NULL || saved_jvms != NULL);
4970 
4971   // The following tests must be performed
4972   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
4973   // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
4974   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4975   // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
4976   // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
4977   // (6) length must not be negative.
4978   // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
4979   // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
4980   // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
4981 
4982   // (3) src and dest must not be null.
4983   // always do this here because we need the JVM state for uncommon traps
4984   Node* null_ctl = top();
4985   src  = saved_jvms != NULL ? null_check_oop(src, &null_ctl, true, true) : null_check(src,  T_ARRAY);
4986   assert(null_ctl->is_top(), "no null control here");
4987   dest = null_check(dest, T_ARRAY);
4988 
4989   if (!can_emit_guards) {
4990     // if saved_jvms == NULL and alloc != NULL, we don't emit any
4991     // guards but the arraycopy node could still take advantage of a
4992     // tightly allocated allocation. tightly_coupled_allocation() is
4993     // called again to make sure it takes the null check above into
4994     // account: the null check is mandatory and if it caused an
4995     // uncommon trap to be emitted then the allocation can't be
4996     // considered tightly coupled in this context.
4997     alloc = tightly_coupled_allocation(dest, NULL);
4998   }
4999 
5000   bool validated = false;
5001 
5002   const Type* src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
5003   const Type* dest_type = _gvn.type(dest);
5004   const TypeAryPtr* top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5005   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5006 
5007   // Do we have the type of src?
5008   bool has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
5009   // Do we have the type of dest?
5010   bool has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
5011   // Is the type for src from speculation?
5012   bool src_spec = false;
5013   // Is the type for dest from speculation?
5014   bool dest_spec = false;
5015 
5016   if ((!has_src || !has_dest) && can_emit_guards) {
5017     // We don't have sufficient type information, let's see if
5018     // speculative types can help. We need to have types for both src
5019     // and dest so that it pays off.
5020 
5021     // Do we already have or could we have type information for src
5022     bool could_have_src = has_src;
5023     // Do we already have or could we have type information for dest
5024     bool could_have_dest = has_dest;
5025 
5026     ciKlass* src_k = NULL;
5027     if (!has_src) {
5028       src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5029       if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
5030         could_have_src = true;
5031       }
5032     }
5033 
5034     ciKlass* dest_k = NULL;
5035     if (!has_dest) {
5036       dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5037       if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
5038         could_have_dest = true;
5039       }
5040     }
5041 
5042     if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5043       // This is going to pay off so emit the required guards
5044       if (!has_src) {
5045         src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5046         src_type  = _gvn.type(src);
5047         top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5048         has_src = (top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL);
5049         src_spec = true;
5050       }
5051       if (!has_dest) {
5052         dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5053         dest_type  = _gvn.type(dest);
5054         top_dest  = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
5055         has_dest = (top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL);
5056         dest_spec = true;
5057       }
5058     }
5059   }
5060 
5061   if (has_src && has_dest && can_emit_guards) {
5062     BasicType src_elem  = top_src->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5063     BasicType dest_elem = top_dest->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5064     if (src_elem  == T_ARRAY)  src_elem  = T_OBJECT;
5065     if (dest_elem == T_ARRAY)  dest_elem = T_OBJECT;
5066 
5067     if (src_elem == dest_elem && src_elem == T_OBJECT) {
5068       // If both arrays are object arrays then having the exact types
5069       // for both will remove the need for a subtype check at runtime
5070       // before the call and may make it possible to pick a faster copy
5071       // routine (without a subtype check on every element)
5072       // Do we have the exact type of src?
5073       bool could_have_src = src_spec;
5074       // Do we have the exact type of dest?
5075       bool could_have_dest = dest_spec;
5076       ciKlass* src_k = top_src->klass();
5077       ciKlass* dest_k = top_dest->klass();
5078       if (!src_spec) {
5079         src_k = src_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5080         if (src_k != NULL && src_k->is_array_klass()) {
5081           could_have_src = true;
5082         }
5083       }
5084       if (!dest_spec) {
5085         dest_k = dest_type->speculative_type_not_null();
5086         if (dest_k != NULL && dest_k->is_array_klass()) {
5087           could_have_dest = true;
5088         }
5089       }
5090       if (could_have_src && could_have_dest) {
5091         // If we can have both exact types, emit the missing guards
5092         if (could_have_src && !src_spec) {
5093           src = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(src, src_k, true);
5094         }
5095         if (could_have_dest && !dest_spec) {
5096           dest = maybe_cast_profiled_obj(dest, dest_k, true);
5097         }
5098       }
5099     }
5100   }
5101 
5102   ciMethod* trap_method = method();
5103   int trap_bci = bci();
5104   if (saved_jvms != NULL) {
5105     trap_method = alloc->jvms()->method();
5106     trap_bci = alloc->jvms()->bci();
5107   }
5108 
5109   bool negative_length_guard_generated = false;
5110 
5111   if (!C->too_many_traps(trap_method, trap_bci, Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic) &&
5112       can_emit_guards &&
5113       !src->is_top() && !dest->is_top()) {
5114     // validate arguments: enables transformation the ArrayCopyNode
5115     validated = true;
5116 
5117     RegionNode* slow_region = new RegionNode(1);
5118     record_for_igvn(slow_region);
5119 
5120     // (1) src and dest are arrays.
5121     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(src), slow_region);
5122     generate_non_array_guard(load_object_klass(dest), slow_region);
5123 
5124     // (2) src and dest arrays must have elements of the same BasicType
5125     // done at macro expansion or at Ideal transformation time
5126 
5127     // (4) src_offset must not be negative.
5128     generate_negative_guard(src_offset, slow_region);
5129 
5130     // (5) dest_offset must not be negative.
5131     generate_negative_guard(dest_offset, slow_region);
5132 
5133     // (7) src_offset + length must not exceed length of src.
5134     generate_limit_guard(src_offset, length,
5135                          load_array_length(src),
5136                          slow_region);
5137 
5138     // (8) dest_offset + length must not exceed length of dest.
5139     generate_limit_guard(dest_offset, length,
5140                          load_array_length(dest),
5141                          slow_region);
5142 
5143     // (6) length must not be negative.
5144     // This is also checked in generate_arraycopy() during macro expansion, but
5145     // we also have to check it here for the case where the ArrayCopyNode will
5146     // be eliminated by Escape Analysis.
5147     if (EliminateAllocations) {
5148       generate_negative_guard(length, slow_region);
5149       negative_length_guard_generated = true;
5150     }
5151 
5152     // (9) each element of an oop array must be assignable
5153     Node* dest_klass = load_object_klass(dest);
5154     if (src != dest) {
5155       Node* not_subtype_ctrl = gen_subtype_check(src, dest_klass);
5156 
5157       if (not_subtype_ctrl != top()) {
5158         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5159         set_control(not_subtype_ctrl);
5160         uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5161                       Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5162         assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5163       }
5164     }
5165 
5166     const TypeKlassPtr* dest_klass_t = _gvn.type(dest_klass)->is_klassptr();
5167     const Type* toop = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(dest_klass_t->klass());
5168     src = _gvn.transform(new CheckCastPPNode(control(), src, toop));
5169     src_type = _gvn.type(src);
5170     top_src  = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5171 
5172     if (top_dest != NULL && !top_dest->elem()->isa_valuetype() && !top_dest->is_not_flat()) {
5173       generate_valueArray_guard(dest_klass, slow_region);
5174     }
5175 
5176     if (top_src != NULL && !top_src->elem()->isa_valuetype() && !top_src->is_not_flat()) {
5177       Node* src_klass = load_object_klass(src);
5178       generate_valueArray_guard(src_klass, slow_region);
5179     }
5180 
5181     {
5182       PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
5183       set_control(_gvn.transform(slow_region));
5184       uncommon_trap(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
5185                     Deoptimization::Action_make_not_entrant);
5186       assert(stopped(), "Should be stopped");
5187     }
5188   }
5189 
5190   arraycopy_move_allocation_here(alloc, dest, saved_jvms, saved_reexecute_sp, new_idx);
5191 
5192   if (stopped()) {
5193     return true;
5194   }
5195 
5196   ArrayCopyNode* ac = ArrayCopyNode::make(this, true, src, src_offset, dest, dest_offset, length, alloc != NULL, negative_length_guard_generated,
5197                                           // Create LoadRange and LoadKlass nodes for use during macro expansion here
5198                                           // so the compiler has a chance to eliminate them: during macro expansion,
5199                                           // we have to set their control (CastPP nodes are eliminated).
5200                                           load_object_klass(src), load_object_klass(dest),
5201                                           load_array_length(src), load_array_length(dest));
5202 
5203   ac->set_arraycopy(validated);
5204 
5205   Node* n = _gvn.transform(ac);
5206   if (n == ac) {
5207     ac->connect_outputs(this);
5208   } else {
5209     assert(validated, "shouldn't transform if all arguments not validated");
5210     set_all_memory(n);
5211   }
5212   clear_upper_avx();
5213 
5214 
5215   return true;
5216 }
5217 
5218 
5219 // Helper function which determines if an arraycopy immediately follows
5220 // an allocation, with no intervening tests or other escapes for the object.
5221 AllocateArrayNode*
5222 LibraryCallKit::tightly_coupled_allocation(Node* ptr,
5223                                            RegionNode* slow_region) {
5224   if (stopped())             return NULL;  // no fast path
5225   if (C->AliasLevel() == 0)  return NULL;  // no MergeMems around
5226 
5227   AllocateArrayNode* alloc = AllocateArrayNode::Ideal_array_allocation(ptr, &_gvn);
5228   if (alloc == NULL)  return NULL;
5229 
5230   Node* rawmem = memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5231   // Is the allocation's memory state untouched?
5232   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0)->is_Initialize())) {
5233     // Bail out if there have been raw-memory effects since the allocation.
5234     // (Example:  There might have been a call or safepoint.)
5235     return NULL;
5236   }
5237   rawmem = rawmem->in(0)->as_Initialize()->memory(Compile::AliasIdxRaw);
5238   if (!(rawmem->is_Proj() && rawmem->in(0) == alloc)) {
5239     return NULL;
5240   }
5241 
5242   // There must be no unexpected observers of this allocation.
5243   for (DUIterator_Fast imax, i = ptr->fast_outs(imax); i < imax; i++) {
5244     Node* obs = ptr->fast_out(i);
5245     if (obs != this->map()) {
5246       return NULL;
5247     }
5248   }
5249 
5250   // This arraycopy must unconditionally follow the allocation of the ptr.
5251   Node* alloc_ctl = ptr->in(0);
5252   Node* ctl = control();
5253   while (ctl != alloc_ctl) {
5254     // There may be guards which feed into the slow_region.
5255     // Any other control flow means that we might not get a chance
5256     // to finish initializing the allocated object.
5257     if ((ctl->is_IfFalse() || ctl->is_IfTrue()) && ctl->in(0)->is_If()) {
5258       IfNode* iff = ctl->in(0)->as_If();
5259       Node* not_ctl = iff->proj_out_or_null(1 - ctl->as_Proj()->_con);
5260       assert(not_ctl != NULL && not_ctl != ctl, "found alternate");
5261       if (slow_region != NULL && slow_region->find_edge(not_ctl) >= 1) {
5262         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds the known slow_region.
5263         continue;
5264       }
5265       // One more try:  Various low-level checks bottom out in
5266       // uncommon traps.  If the debug-info of the trap omits
5267       // any reference to the allocation, as we've already
5268       // observed, then there can be no objection to the trap.
5269       bool found_trap = false;
5270       for (DUIterator_Fast jmax, j = not_ctl->fast_outs(jmax); j < jmax; j++) {
5271         Node* obs = not_ctl->fast_out(j);
5272         if (obs->in(0) == not_ctl && obs->is_Call() &&
5273             (obs->as_Call()->entry_point() == SharedRuntime::uncommon_trap_blob()->entry_point())) {
5274           found_trap = true; break;
5275         }
5276       }
5277       if (found_trap) {
5278         ctl = iff->in(0);       // This test feeds a harmless uncommon trap.
5279         continue;
5280       }
5281     }
5282     return NULL;
5283   }
5284 
5285   // If we get this far, we have an allocation which immediately
5286   // precedes the arraycopy, and we can take over zeroing the new object.
5287   // The arraycopy will finish the initialization, and provide
5288   // a new control state to which we will anchor the destination pointer.
5289 
5290   return alloc;
5291 }
5292 
5293 //-------------inline_encodeISOArray-----------------------------------
5294 // encode char[] to byte[] in ISO_8859_1
5295 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_encodeISOArray() {
5296   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "encodeISOArray has 5 parameters");
5297   // no receiver since it is static method
5298   Node *src         = argument(0);
5299   Node *src_offset  = argument(1);
5300   Node *dst         = argument(2);
5301   Node *dst_offset  = argument(3);
5302   Node *length      = argument(4);
5303 
5304   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5305   dst = must_be_not_null(dst, true);
5306 
5307   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5308   const Type* dst_type = dst->Value(&_gvn);
5309   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5310   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dst_type->isa_aryptr();
5311   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL ||
5312       top_dest == NULL || top_dest->klass() == NULL) {
5313     // failed array check
5314     return false;
5315   }
5316 
5317   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5318   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5319   BasicType dst_elem = dst_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5320   if (!((src_elem == T_CHAR) || (src_elem== T_BYTE)) || dst_elem != T_BYTE) {
5321     return false;
5322   }
5323 
5324   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_CHAR);
5325   Node* dst_start = array_element_address(dst, dst_offset, dst_elem);
5326   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5327   // 'dst_start' points to dst array + scaled offset
5328 
5329   const TypeAryPtr* mtype = TypeAryPtr::BYTES;
5330   Node* enc = new EncodeISOArrayNode(control(), memory(mtype), src_start, dst_start, length);
5331   enc = _gvn.transform(enc);
5332   Node* res_mem = _gvn.transform(new SCMemProjNode(enc));
5333   set_memory(res_mem, mtype);
5334   set_result(enc);
5335   clear_upper_avx();
5336 
5337   return true;
5338 }
5339 
5340 //-------------inline_multiplyToLen-----------------------------------
5341 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_multiplyToLen() {
5342   assert(UseMultiplyToLenIntrinsic, "not implemented on this platform");
5343 
5344   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::multiplyToLen();
5345   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5346     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5347   }
5348   const char* stubName = "multiplyToLen";
5349 
5350   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "multiplyToLen has 5 parameters");
5351 
5352   // no receiver because it is a static method
5353   Node* x    = argument(0);
5354   Node* xlen = argument(1);
5355   Node* y    = argument(2);
5356   Node* ylen = argument(3);
5357   Node* z    = argument(4);
5358 
5359   x = must_be_not_null(x, true);
5360   y = must_be_not_null(y, true);
5361 
5362   const Type* x_type = x->Value(&_gvn);
5363   const Type* y_type = y->Value(&_gvn);
5364   const TypeAryPtr* top_x = x_type->isa_aryptr();
5365   const TypeAryPtr* top_y = y_type->isa_aryptr();
5366   if (top_x  == NULL || top_x->klass()  == NULL ||
5367       top_y == NULL || top_y->klass() == NULL) {
5368     // failed array check
5369     return false;
5370   }
5371 
5372   BasicType x_elem = x_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5373   BasicType y_elem = y_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5374   if (x_elem != T_INT || y_elem != T_INT) {
5375     return false;
5376   }
5377 
5378   // Set the original stack and the reexecute bit for the interpreter to reexecute
5379   // the bytecode that invokes BigInteger.multiplyToLen() if deoptimization happens
5380   // on the return from z array allocation in runtime.
5381   { PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
5382     jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
5383 
5384     Node* x_start = array_element_address(x, intcon(0), x_elem);
5385     Node* y_start = array_element_address(y, intcon(0), y_elem);
5386     // 'x_start' points to x array + scaled xlen
5387     // 'y_start' points to y array + scaled ylen
5388 
5389     // Allocate the result array
5390     Node* zlen = _gvn.transform(new AddINode(xlen, ylen));
5391     ciKlass* klass = ciTypeArrayKlass::make(T_INT);
5392     Node* klass_node = makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(klass));
5393 
5394     IdealKit ideal(this);
5395 
5396 #define __ ideal.
5397      Node* one = __ ConI(1);
5398      Node* zero = __ ConI(0);
5399      IdealVariable need_alloc(ideal), z_alloc(ideal);  __ declarations_done();
5400      __ set(need_alloc, zero);
5401      __ set(z_alloc, z);
5402      __ if_then(z, BoolTest::eq, null()); {
5403        __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5404      } __ else_(); {
5405        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5406        sync_kit(ideal);
5407        Node *cast = new CastPPNode(z, TypePtr::NOTNULL);
5408        cast->init_req(0, control());
5409        _gvn.set_type(cast, cast->bottom_type());
5410        C->record_for_igvn(cast);
5411 
5412        Node* zlen_arg = load_array_length(cast);
5413        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5414        __ sync_kit(this);
5415        __ if_then(zlen_arg, BoolTest::lt, zlen); {
5416          __ increment (need_alloc, one);
5417        } __ end_if();
5418      } __ end_if();
5419 
5420      __ if_then(__ value(need_alloc), BoolTest::ne, zero); {
5421        // Update graphKit memory and control from IdealKit.
5422        sync_kit(ideal);
5423        Node * narr = new_array(klass_node, zlen, 1);
5424        // Update IdealKit memory and control from graphKit.
5425        __ sync_kit(this);
5426        __ set(z_alloc, narr);
5427      } __ end_if();
5428 
5429      sync_kit(ideal);
5430      z = __ value(z_alloc);
5431      // Can't use TypeAryPtr::INTS which uses Bottom offset.
5432      _gvn.set_type(z, TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass));
5433      // Final sync IdealKit and GraphKit.
5434      final_sync(ideal);
5435 #undef __
5436 
5437     Node* z_start = array_element_address(z, intcon(0), T_INT);
5438 
5439     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
5440                                    OptoRuntime::multiplyToLen_Type(),
5441                                    stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5442                                    x_start, xlen, y_start, ylen, z_start, zlen);
5443   } // original reexecute is set back here
5444 
5445   C->set_has_split_ifs(true); // Has chance for split-if optimization
5446   set_result(z);
5447   return true;
5448 }

5585   BasicType b_elem = b_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();

5664 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_bigIntegerShift(bool isRightShift) {
5665   address stubAddr = NULL;
5666   const char* stubName = NULL;
5667 
5668   stubAddr = isRightShift? StubRoutines::bigIntegerRightShift(): StubRoutines::bigIntegerLeftShift();
5669   if (stubAddr == NULL) {
5670     return false; // Intrinsic's stub is not implemented on this platform
5671   }
5672 
5673   stubName = isRightShift? "bigIntegerRightShiftWorker" : "bigIntegerLeftShiftWorker";
5674 
5675   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "expected 5 arguments");
5676 
5677   Node* newArr = argument(0);
5678   Node* oldArr = argument(1);
5679   Node* newIdx = argument(2);
5680   Node* shiftCount = argument(3);
5681   Node* numIter = argument(4);
5682 
5683   const Type* newArr_type = newArr->Value(&_gvn);
5684   const TypeAryPtr* top_newArr = newArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5685   const Type* oldArr_type = oldArr->Value(&_gvn);
5686   const TypeAryPtr* top_oldArr = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr();
5687   if (top_newArr == NULL || top_newArr->klass() == NULL || top_oldArr == NULL
5688       || top_oldArr->klass() == NULL) {
5689     return false;
5690   }
5691 
5692   BasicType newArr_elem = newArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5693   BasicType oldArr_elem = oldArr_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5694   if (newArr_elem != T_INT || oldArr_elem != T_INT) {
5695     return false;
5696   }
5697 
5698   // Make the call
5699   {
5700     Node* newArr_start = array_element_address(newArr, intcon(0), newArr_elem);
5701     Node* oldArr_start = array_element_address(oldArr, intcon(0), oldArr_elem);
5702 
5703     Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF,
5704                                    OptoRuntime::bigIntegerShift_Type(),
5705                                    stubAddr,
5706                                    stubName,
5707                                    TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5708                                    newArr_start,
5709                                    oldArr_start,
5710                                    newIdx,
5711                                    shiftCount,
5712                                    numIter);
5713   }
5714 
5715   return true;
5716 }

5763 /**
5764  * Calculate CRC32 for byte.
5765  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.update(int crc, int b)
5766  */
5767 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateCRC32() {
5768   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5769   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "update has 2 parameters");
5770   // no receiver since it is static method
5771   Node* crc  = argument(0); // type: int
5772   Node* b    = argument(1); // type: int
5773 
5774   /*
5775    *    int c = ~ crc;
5776    *    b = timesXtoThe32[(b ^ c) & 0xFF];
5777    *    b = b ^ (c >>> 8);
5778    *    crc = ~b;
5779    */
5780 
5781   Node* M1 = intcon(-1);
5782   crc = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, M1));
5783   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, b));
5784   result = _gvn.transform(new AndINode(result, intcon(0xFF)));
5785 
5786   Node* base = makecon(TypeRawPtr::make(StubRoutines::crc_table_addr()));
5787   Node* offset = _gvn.transform(new LShiftINode(result, intcon(0x2)));
5788   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, ConvI2X(offset));
5789   result = make_load(control(), adr, TypeInt::INT, T_INT, MemNode::unordered);
5790 
5791   crc = _gvn.transform(new URShiftINode(crc, intcon(8)));
5792   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(crc, result));
5793   result = _gvn.transform(new XorINode(result, M1));
5794   set_result(result);
5795   return true;
5796 }
5797 
5798 /**
5799  * Calculate CRC32 for byte[] array.
5800  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int len)
5801  */
5802 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32() {
5803   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5804   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5805   // no receiver since it is static method
5806   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5807   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5808   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5809   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int
5810 
5811   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5812   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5813   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5814     // failed array check
5815     return false;
5816   }
5817 
5818   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5819   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5820   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5821     return false;
5822   }
5823 
5824   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5825   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5826   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5827 
5828   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
5829   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
5830 
5831   // Call the stub.
5832   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5833   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5834 
5835   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5836                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5837                                  crc, src_start, length);
5838   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5839   set_result(result);
5840   return true;
5841 }

5843 /**
5844  * Calculate CRC32 for ByteBuffer.
5845  * int java.util.zip.CRC32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
5846  */
5847 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferCRC32() {
5848   assert(UseCRC32Intrinsics, "need AVX and LCMUL instructions support");
5849   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
5850   // no receiver since it is static method
5851   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5852   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
5853   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
5854   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
5855 
5856   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
5857   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
5858   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
5859 
5860   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5861   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
5862 
5863   // Call the stub.
5864   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32();
5865   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32";
5866 
5867   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32_Type(),
5868                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5869                                  crc, src_start, length);
5870   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5871   set_result(result);
5872   return true;
5873 }

5875 //------------------------------get_table_from_crc32c_class-----------------------
5876 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_table_from_crc32c_class(ciInstanceKlass *crc32c_class) {
5877   Node* table = load_field_from_object(NULL, "byteTable", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false, /*is_static*/ true, crc32c_class);
5878   assert (table != NULL, "wrong version of java.util.zip.CRC32C");
5879 
5880   return table;
5881 }
