5883 //------------------------------inline_updateBytesCRC32C-----------------------
5884 //
5885 // Calculate CRC32C for byte[] array.
5886 // int java.util.zip.CRC32C.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int end)
5887 //
5888 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesCRC32C() {
5889   assert(UseCRC32CIntrinsics, "need CRC32C instruction support");
5890   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5891   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "CRC32C class must be loaded");
5892   // no receiver since it is a static method
5893   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5894   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5895   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5896   Node* end     = argument(3); // type: int
5897 
5898   Node* length = _gvn.transform(new SubINode(end, offset));
5899 
5900   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5901   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5902   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5903     // failed array check
5904     return false;
5905   }
5906 
5907   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
5908   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
5909   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
5910     return false;
5911   }
5912 
5913   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
5914   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
5915   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
5916

5930                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,

5933   set_result(result);
5934   return true;

5937 //------------------------------inline_updateDirectByteBufferCRC32C-----------------------

5940 // int java.util.zip.CRC32C.updateDirectByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int end)
5941 //
5942 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateDirectByteBufferCRC32C() {
5943   assert(UseCRC32CIntrinsics, "need CRC32C instruction support");
5944   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateDirectByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
5945   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "CRC32C class must be loaded");
5946   // no receiver since it is a static method

5949   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int

5960 
5961   // static final int[] byteTable in class CRC32C
5962   Node* table = get_table_from_crc32c_class(callee()->holder());
5963   table = must_be_not_null(table, true);
5964   Node* table_start = array_element_address(table, intcon(0), T_INT);
5965 
5966   // Call the stub.
5967   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesCRC32C();
5968   const char *stubName = "updateBytesCRC32C";
5969 
5970   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesCRC32C_Type(),
5971                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
5972                                  crc, src_start, length, table_start);
5973   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
5974   set_result(result);
5975   return true;
5976 }
5977 
5978 //------------------------------inline_updateBytesAdler32----------------------
5979 //
5980 // Calculate Adler32 checksum for byte[] array.
5981 // int java.util.zip.Adler32.updateBytes(int crc, byte[] buf, int off, int len)
5982 //
5983 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateBytesAdler32() {
5984   assert(UseAdler32Intrinsics, "Adler32 Instrinsic support need"); // check if we actually need to check this flag or check a different one
5985   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "updateBytes has 4 parameters");
5986   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "Adler32 class must be loaded");
5987   // no receiver since it is static method
5988   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
5989   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: oop
5990   Node* offset  = argument(2); // type: int
5991   Node* length  = argument(3); // type: int
5992 
5993   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
5994   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
5995   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
5996     // failed array check
5997     return false;
5998   }
5999 
6000   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6001   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6002   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6003     return false;
6004   }
6005 
6006   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
6007   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, offset, src_elem);
6008 
6009   // We assume that range check is done by caller.
6010   // TODO: generate range check (offset+length < src.length) in debug VM.
6011 
6012   // Call the stub.
6013   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
6014   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
6015 
6016   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
6017                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6018                                  crc, src_start, length);
6019   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6020   set_result(result);
6021   return true;
6022 }
6023 
6024 //------------------------------inline_updateByteBufferAdler32---------------
6025 //
6026 // Calculate Adler32 checksum for DirectByteBuffer.
6027 // int java.util.zip.Adler32.updateByteBuffer(int crc, long buf, int off, int len)
6028 //
6029 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_updateByteBufferAdler32() {
6030   assert(UseAdler32Intrinsics, "Adler32 Instrinsic support need"); // check if we actually need to check this flag or check a different one
6031   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 5, "updateByteBuffer has 4 parameters and one is long");
6032   assert(callee()->holder()->is_loaded(), "Adler32 class must be loaded");
6033   // no receiver since it is static method
6034   Node* crc     = argument(0); // type: int
6035   Node* src     = argument(1); // type: long
6036   Node* offset  = argument(3); // type: int
6037   Node* length  = argument(4); // type: int
6038 
6039   src = ConvL2X(src);  // adjust Java long to machine word
6040   Node* base = _gvn.transform(new CastX2PNode(src));
6041   offset = ConvI2X(offset);
6042 
6043   // 'src_start' points to src array + scaled offset
6044   Node* src_start = basic_plus_adr(top(), base, offset);
6045 
6046   // Call the stub.
6047   address stubAddr = StubRoutines::updateBytesAdler32();
6048   const char *stubName = "updateBytesAdler32";
6049 
6050   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF, OptoRuntime::updateBytesAdler32_Type(),
6051                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6052                                  crc, src_start, length);
6053 
6054   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6055   set_result(result);
6056   return true;
6057 }
6058 
6059 //----------------------------inline_reference_get----------------------------
6060 // public T java.lang.ref.Reference.get();
6061 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_reference_get() {
6062   const int referent_offset = java_lang_ref_Reference::referent_offset;
6063   guarantee(referent_offset > 0, "should have already been set");
6064 
6065   // Get the argument:
6066   Node* reference_obj = null_check_receiver();
6067   if (stopped()) return true;
6068 
6069   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(reference_obj)->isa_instptr();
6070   assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6071   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6072   ciInstanceKlass* referenceKlass = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6073   ciField* field = referenceKlass->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make("referent"),
6074                                                      ciSymbol::make("Ljava/lang/Object;"),
6075                                                      false);
6076   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6077 
6078   Node* adr = basic_plus_adr(reference_obj, reference_obj, referent_offset);
6079   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6080 
6081   ciInstanceKlass* klass = env()->Object_klass();
6082   const TypeOopPtr* object_type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(klass);
6083 
6084   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP | ON_WEAK_OOP_REF;
6085   Node* result = access_load_at(reference_obj, adr, adr_type, object_type, T_OBJECT, decorators);
6086   // Add memory barrier to prevent commoning reads from this field
6087   // across safepoint since GC can change its value.
6088   insert_mem_bar(Op_MemBarCPUOrder);
6089 
6090   set_result(result);
6091   return true;
6092 }
6093 
6094 
6095 Node * LibraryCallKit::load_field_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6096                                               bool is_exact=true, bool is_static=false,
6097                                               ciInstanceKlass * fromKls=NULL) {
6098   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6099     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6100     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6101     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6102     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6103     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6104   } else {
6105     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6106   }
6107   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6108                                               ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6109                                               is_static);
6110 
6111   assert (field != NULL, "undefined field");
6112   if (field == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6113 
6114   if (is_static) {
6115     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6116     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6117   }
6118 
6119   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6120 
6121   // Compute address and memory type.
6122   int offset  = field->offset_in_bytes();
6123   bool is_vol = field->is_volatile();
6124   ciType* field_klass = field->type();
6125   assert(field_klass->is_loaded(), "should be loaded");
6126   const TypePtr* adr_type = C->alias_type(field)->adr_type();
6127   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6128   BasicType bt = field->layout_type();
6129 
6130   // Build the resultant type of the load
6131   const Type *type;
6132   if (bt == T_OBJECT) {
6133     type = TypeOopPtr::make_from_klass(field_klass->as_klass());
6134   } else {
6135     type = Type::get_const_basic_type(bt);
6136   }
6137 
6138   DecoratorSet decorators = IN_HEAP;
6139 
6140   if (is_vol) {
6141     decorators |= MO_SEQ_CST;
6142   }
6143 
6144   return access_load_at(fromObj, adr, adr_type, type, bt, decorators);
6145 }
6146 
6147 Node * LibraryCallKit::field_address_from_object(Node * fromObj, const char * fieldName, const char * fieldTypeString,
6148                                                  bool is_exact = true, bool is_static = false,
6149                                                  ciInstanceKlass * fromKls = NULL) {
6150   if (fromKls == NULL) {
6151     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(fromObj)->isa_instptr();
6152     assert(tinst != NULL, "obj is null");
6153     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "obj is not loaded");
6154     assert(!is_exact || tinst->klass_is_exact(), "klass not exact");
6155     fromKls = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass();
6156   }
6157   else {
6158     assert(is_static, "only for static field access");
6159   }
6160   ciField* field = fromKls->get_field_by_name(ciSymbol::make(fieldName),
6161     ciSymbol::make(fieldTypeString),
6162     is_static);
6163 
6164   assert(field != NULL, "undefined field");
6165   assert(!field->is_volatile(), "not defined for volatile fields");
6166 
6167   if (is_static) {
6168     const TypeInstPtr* tip = TypeInstPtr::make(fromKls->java_mirror());
6169     fromObj = makecon(tip);
6170   }
6171 
6172   // Next code  copied from Parse::do_get_xxx():
6173 
6174   // Compute address and memory type.
6175   int offset = field->offset_in_bytes();
6176   Node *adr = basic_plus_adr(fromObj, fromObj, offset);
6177 
6178   return adr;
6179 }

6181 //------------------------------inline_aescrypt_Block-----------------------
6182 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_aescrypt_Block(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6183   address stubAddr = NULL;
6184   const char *stubName;
6185   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6186 
6187   switch(id) {
6188   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_encryptBlock:
6189     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_encryptBlock();
6190     stubName = "aescrypt_encryptBlock";
6191     break;
6192   case vmIntrinsics::_aescrypt_decryptBlock:
6193     stubAddr = StubRoutines::aescrypt_decryptBlock();
6194     stubName = "aescrypt_decryptBlock";
6195     break;
6196   default:
6197     break;
6198   }
6199   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6200 
6201   Node* aescrypt_object = argument(0);
6202   Node* src             = argument(1);
6203   Node* src_offset      = argument(2);
6204   Node* dest            = argument(3);
6205   Node* dest_offset     = argument(4);
6206 
6207   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6208   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6209 
6210   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6211   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6212   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6213   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6214   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6215   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6216 
6217   // for the quick and dirty code we will skip all the checks.
6218   // we are just trying to get the call to be generated.
6219   Node* src_start  = src;
6220   Node* dest_start = dest;
6221   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6222     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6223     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6224     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6225   }
6226 
6227   // now need to get the start of its expanded key array
6228   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6229   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6230   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6231 
6232   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6233     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6234     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6235     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6236     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6237 
6238     // Call the stub.
6239     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6240                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6241                       src_start, dest_start, k_start, original_k_start);
6242   } else {
6243     // Call the stub.
6244     make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::aescrypt_block_Type(),
6245                       stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6246                       src_start, dest_start, k_start);
6247   }
6248 
6249   return true;
6250 }
6251 
6252 //------------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt-----------------------
6253 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6254   address stubAddr = NULL;
6255   const char *stubName = NULL;
6256 
6257   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6258 
6259   switch(id) {
6260   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt:
6261     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt();
6262     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt";
6263     break;
6264   case vmIntrinsics::_cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt:
6265     stubAddr = StubRoutines::cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt();
6266     stubName = "cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt";
6267     break;
6268   default:
6269     break;
6270   }
6271   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6272 
6273   Node* cipherBlockChaining_object = argument(0);
6274   Node* src                        = argument(1);
6275   Node* src_offset                 = argument(2);
6276   Node* len                        = argument(3);
6277   Node* dest                       = argument(4);
6278   Node* dest_offset                = argument(5);
6279 
6280   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6281   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, false);
6282 
6283   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6284   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6285   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6286   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6287   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6288   assert (top_src  != NULL && top_src->klass()  != NULL
6289           &&  top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6290 
6291   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
6292   Node* src_start  = src;
6293   Node* dest_start = dest;
6294   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6295     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6296     src_start  = array_element_address(src,  src_offset,  T_BYTE);
6297     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6298   }
6299 
6300   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
6301   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
6302   // so we cast it here safely.
6303   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6304 
6305   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6306   if (embeddedCipherObj == NULL) return false;
6307 
6308   // cast it to what we know it will be at runtime
6309   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(cipherBlockChaining_object)->isa_instptr();
6310   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBC obj is null");
6311   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBC obj is not loaded");
6312   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6313   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6314 
6315   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6316   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6317   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6318   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6319   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6320 
6321   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6322   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6323   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6324 
6325   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6326   Node* objRvec = load_field_from_object(cipherBlockChaining_object, "r", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6327   if (objRvec == NULL) return false;
6328   Node* r_start = array_element_address(objRvec, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6329 
6330   Node* cbcCrypt;
6331   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6332     // on SPARC we need to pass the original key since key expansion needs to happen in intrinsics due to
6333     // compatibility issues between Java key expansion and SPARC crypto instructions
6334     Node* original_k_start = get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6335     if (original_k_start == NULL) return false;
6336 
6337     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, src_len and original_k_start
6338     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6339                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6340                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6341                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len, original_k_start);
6342   } else {
6343     // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6344     cbcCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6345                                  OptoRuntime::cipherBlockChaining_aescrypt_Type(),
6346                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6347                                  src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start, len);
6348   }
6349 
6350   // return cipher length (int)
6351   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(cbcCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6352   set_result(retvalue);
6353   return true;
6354 }

6444 //------------------------------inline_counterMode_AESCrypt-----------------------
6445 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_counterMode_AESCrypt(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6446   assert(UseAES, "need AES instruction support");
6447   if (!UseAESCTRIntrinsics) return false;
6448 
6449   address stubAddr = NULL;
6450   const char *stubName = NULL;
6451   if (id == vmIntrinsics::_counterMode_AESCrypt) {
6452     stubAddr = StubRoutines::counterMode_AESCrypt();
6453     stubName = "counterMode_AESCrypt";
6454   }
6455   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6456 
6457   Node* counterMode_object = argument(0);
6458   Node* src = argument(1);
6459   Node* src_offset = argument(2);
6460   Node* len = argument(3);
6461   Node* dest = argument(4);
6462   Node* dest_offset = argument(5);
6463 
6464   // (1) src and dest are arrays.
6465   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6466   const Type* dest_type = dest->Value(&_gvn);
6467   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6468   const TypeAryPtr* top_dest = dest_type->isa_aryptr();
6469   assert(top_src != NULL && top_src->klass() != NULL &&
6470          top_dest != NULL && top_dest->klass() != NULL, "args are strange");
6471 
6472   // checks are the responsibility of the caller
6473   Node* src_start = src;
6474   Node* dest_start = dest;
6475   if (src_offset != NULL || dest_offset != NULL) {
6476     assert(src_offset != NULL && dest_offset != NULL, "");
6477     src_start = array_element_address(src, src_offset, T_BYTE);
6478     dest_start = array_element_address(dest, dest_offset, T_BYTE);
6479   }
6480 
6481   // if we are in this set of code, we "know" the embeddedCipher is an AESCrypt object
6482   // (because of the predicated logic executed earlier).
6483   // so we cast it here safely.
6484   // this requires a newer class file that has this array as littleEndian ints, otherwise we revert to java
6485   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6486   if (embeddedCipherObj == NULL) return false;
6487   // cast it to what we know it will be at runtime
6488   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(counterMode_object)->isa_instptr();
6489   assert(tinst != NULL, "CTR obj is null");
6490   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CTR obj is not loaded");
6491   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6492   assert(klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6493   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6494   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt);
6495   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6496   Node* aescrypt_object = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), embeddedCipherObj, xtype);
6497   aescrypt_object = _gvn.transform(aescrypt_object);
6498   // we need to get the start of the aescrypt_object's expanded key array
6499   Node* k_start = get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(aescrypt_object);
6500   if (k_start == NULL) return false;
6501   // similarly, get the start address of the r vector
6502   Node* obj_counter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "counter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6503   if (obj_counter == NULL) return false;
6504   Node* cnt_start = array_element_address(obj_counter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6505 
6506   Node* saved_encCounter = load_field_from_object(counterMode_object, "encryptedCounter", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6507   if (saved_encCounter == NULL) return false;
6508   Node* saved_encCounter_start = array_element_address(saved_encCounter, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6509   Node* used = field_address_from_object(counterMode_object, "used", "I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6510 
6511   Node* ctrCrypt;
6512   if (Matcher::pass_original_key_for_aes()) {
6513     // no SPARC version for AES/CTR intrinsics now.
6514     return false;
6515   }
6516   // Call the stub, passing src_start, dest_start, k_start, r_start and src_len
6517   ctrCrypt = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6518                                OptoRuntime::counterMode_aescrypt_Type(),
6519                                stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6520                                src_start, dest_start, k_start, cnt_start, len, saved_encCounter_start, used);
6521 
6522   // return cipher length (int)
6523   Node* retvalue = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(ctrCrypt, TypeFunc::Parms));
6524   set_result(retvalue);
6525   return true;
6526 }
6527 
6528 //------------------------------get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6529 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6530 #if defined(PPC64) || defined(S390)
6531   // MixColumns for decryption can be reduced by preprocessing MixColumns with round keys.
6532   // Intel's extention is based on this optimization and AESCrypt generates round keys by preprocessing MixColumns.
6533   // However, ppc64 vncipher processes MixColumns and requires the same round keys with encryption.
6534   // The ppc64 stubs of encryption and decryption use the same round keys (sessionK[0]).
6535   Node* objSessionK = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "sessionK", "[[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6536   assert (objSessionK != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6537   if (objSessionK == NULL) {
6538     return (Node *) NULL;
6539   }
6540   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_array_element(control(), objSessionK, intcon(0), TypeAryPtr::OOPS);
6541 #else
6542   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "K", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6543 #endif // PPC64
6544   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6545   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6546 
6547   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the K array
6548   Node* k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_INT);
6549   return k_start;
6550 }
6551 
6552 //------------------------------get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object-----------------------
6553 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_original_key_start_from_aescrypt_object(Node *aescrypt_object) {
6554   Node* objAESCryptKey = load_field_from_object(aescrypt_object, "lastKey", "[B", /*is_exact*/ false);
6555   assert (objAESCryptKey != NULL, "wrong version of com.sun.crypto.provider.AESCrypt");
6556   if (objAESCryptKey == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6557 
6558   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the lastKey array
6559   Node* original_k_start = array_element_address(objAESCryptKey, intcon(0), T_BYTE);
6560   return original_k_start;
6561 }
6562 
6563 //----------------------------inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6564 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6565 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6566 // for encryption:
6567 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6568 // for decryption:
6569 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6570 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6571 //
6572 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_cipherBlockChaining_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6573   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6574   Node* objCBC = argument(0);
6575 
6576   Node* src = argument(1);
6577   Node* dest = argument(4);
6578 
6579   // Load embeddedCipher field of CipherBlockChaining object.
6580   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objCBC, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6581 
6582   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check
6583   // AESCrypt might not be loaded yet if some other SymmetricCipher got us to this compile point
6584   // will have same classloader as CipherBlockChaining object
6585   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(objCBC)->isa_instptr();
6586   assert(tinst != NULL, "CBCobj is null");
6587   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "CBCobj is not loaded");
6588 
6589   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6590   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6591   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6592     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6593     Node* ctrl = control();
6594     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6595     return ctrl;
6596   }
6597 
6598   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6599   dest = must_be_not_null(dest, true);
6600 
6601   // Resolve oops to stable for CmpP below.
6602   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6603 
6604   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6605   Node* cmp_instof  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6606   Node* bool_instof  = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6607 
6608   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6609 
6610   // for encryption, we are done
6611   if (!decrypting)
6612     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6613 
6614   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6615   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6616   // see the original java code for why.
6617   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6618   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6619 
6620   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6621   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6622   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6623   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6624 
6625   record_for_igvn(region);
6626   return _gvn.transform(region);
6627 }
6628 
6629 //----------------------------inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate----------------------------
6630 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6631 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6632 // for encryption:
6633 //    if (embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6634 // for decryption:
6635 //    if ((embeddedCipherObj instanceof AESCrypt) && (cipher!=plain)) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
6636 //    note cipher==plain is more conservative than the original java code but that's OK
6637 //
6638 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_electronicCodeBook_AESCrypt_predicate(bool decrypting) {
6639   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6640   Node* objECB = argument(0);
6641 
6642   // Load embeddedCipher field of ElectronicCodeBook object.
6643   Node* embeddedCipherObj = load_field_from_object(objECB, "embeddedCipher", "Lcom/sun/crypto/provider/SymmetricCipher;", /*is_exact*/ false);
6644 
6645   // get AESCrypt klass for instanceOf check
6646   // AESCrypt might not be loaded yet if some other SymmetricCipher got us to this compile point
6647   // will have same classloader as ElectronicCodeBook object
6648   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(objECB)->isa_instptr();
6649   assert(tinst != NULL, "ECBobj is null");
6650   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "ECBobj is not loaded");
6651 
6652   // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the AESCrypt class
6653   ciKlass* klass_AESCrypt = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make("com/sun/crypto/provider/AESCrypt"));
6654   if (!klass_AESCrypt->is_loaded()) {
6655     // if AESCrypt is not even loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
6656     Node* ctrl = control();
6657     set_control(top()); // no regular fast path
6658     return ctrl;
6659   }
6660   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_AESCrypt = klass_AESCrypt->as_instance_klass();
6661 
6662   Node* instof = gen_instanceof(embeddedCipherObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_AESCrypt)));
6663   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instof, intcon(1)));
6664   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
6665 
6666   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6667 
6668   // for encryption, we are done
6669   if (!decrypting)
6670     return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
6671 
6672   // for decryption, we need to add a further check to avoid
6673   // taking the intrinsic path when cipher and plain are the same
6674   // see the original java code for why.
6675   RegionNode* region = new RegionNode(3);
6676   region->init_req(1, instof_false);
6677   Node* src = argument(1);
6678   Node* dest = argument(4);
6679   Node* cmp_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new CmpPNode(src, dest));
6680   Node* bool_src_dest = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_src_dest, BoolTest::eq));
6681   Node* src_dest_conjoint = generate_guard(bool_src_dest, NULL, PROB_MIN);
6682   region->init_req(2, src_dest_conjoint);
6683 
6684   record_for_igvn(region);
6685   return _gvn.transform(region);
6686 }

6730 //------------------------------inline_ghash_processBlocks
6731 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_ghash_processBlocks() {
6732   address stubAddr;
6733   const char *stubName;
6734   assert(UseGHASHIntrinsics, "need GHASH intrinsics support");
6735 
6736   stubAddr = StubRoutines::ghash_processBlocks();
6737   stubName = "ghash_processBlocks";
6738 
6739   Node* data           = argument(0);
6740   Node* offset         = argument(1);
6741   Node* len            = argument(2);
6742   Node* state          = argument(3);
6743   Node* subkeyH        = argument(4);
6744 
6745   state = must_be_not_null(state, true);
6746   subkeyH = must_be_not_null(subkeyH, true);
6747   data = must_be_not_null(data, true);
6748 
6749   Node* state_start  = array_element_address(state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6750   assert(state_start, "state is NULL");
6751   Node* subkeyH_start  = array_element_address(subkeyH, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6752   assert(subkeyH_start, "subkeyH is NULL");
6753   Node* data_start  = array_element_address(data, offset, T_BYTE);
6754   assert(data_start, "data is NULL");
6755 
6756   Node* ghash = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6757                                   OptoRuntime::ghash_processBlocks_Type(),
6758                                   stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6759                                   state_start, subkeyH_start, data_start, len);
6760   return true;
6761 }

6795 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompress-----------------------
6796 //
6797 // Calculate SHA (i.e., SHA-1) for single-block byte[] array.
6798 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6799 //
6800 // Calculate SHA2 (i.e., SHA-244 or SHA-256) for single-block byte[] array.
6801 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA2.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6802 //
6803 // Calculate SHA5 (i.e., SHA-384 or SHA-512) for single-block byte[] array.
6804 // void com.sun.security.provider.SHA5.implCompress(byte[] buf, int ofs)
6805 //
6806 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompress(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
6807   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "sha_implCompress has 2 parameters");
6808 
6809   Node* sha_obj = argument(0);
6810   Node* src     = argument(1); // type oop
6811   Node* ofs     = argument(2); // type int
6812 
6813   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6814   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6815   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6816     // failed array check
6817     return false;
6818   }
6819   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6820   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6821   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6822     return false;
6823   }
6824   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6825   src = must_be_not_null(src, true);
6826   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6827   Node* state = NULL;
6828   address stubAddr;
6829   const char *stubName;
6830 
6831   switch(id) {
6832   case vmIntrinsics::_sha_implCompress:
6833     assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics, "need SHA1 instruction support");
6834     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6835     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompress();
6836     stubName = "sha1_implCompress";
6837     break;
6838   case vmIntrinsics::_sha2_implCompress:
6839     assert(UseSHA256Intrinsics, "need SHA256 instruction support");
6840     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6841     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompress();
6842     stubName = "sha256_implCompress";
6843     break;
6844   case vmIntrinsics::_sha5_implCompress:
6845     assert(UseSHA512Intrinsics, "need SHA512 instruction support");
6846     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6847     stubAddr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompress();
6848     stubName = "sha512_implCompress";
6849     break;
6850   default:
6851     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
6852     return false;
6853   }
6854   if (state == NULL) return false;
6855 
6856   assert(stubAddr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6857   if (stubAddr == NULL) return false;
6858 
6859   // Call the stub.
6860   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP, OptoRuntime::sha_implCompress_Type(),
6861                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6862                                  src_start, state);
6863 
6864   return true;
6865 }
6866 
6867 //------------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB-----------------------
6868 //
6869 // Calculate SHA/SHA2/SHA5 for multi-block byte[] array.
6870 // int com.sun.security.provider.DigestBase.implCompressMultiBlock(byte[] b, int ofs, int limit)
6871 //
6872 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB(int predicate) {
6873   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
6874          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
6875   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
6876   assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "digestBase_implCompressMB has 3 parameters");
6877 
6878   Node* digestBase_obj = argument(0); // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
6879   Node* src            = argument(1); // byte[] array
6880   Node* ofs            = argument(2); // type int
6881   Node* limit          = argument(3); // type int
6882 
6883   const Type* src_type = src->Value(&_gvn);
6884   const TypeAryPtr* top_src = src_type->isa_aryptr();
6885   if (top_src  == NULL || top_src->klass()  == NULL) {
6886     // failed array check
6887     return false;
6888   }
6889   // Figure out the size and type of the elements we will be copying.
6890   BasicType src_elem = src_type->isa_aryptr()->klass()->as_array_klass()->element_type()->basic_type();
6891   if (src_elem != T_BYTE) {
6892     return false;
6893   }
6894   // 'src_start' points to src array + offset
6895   src = must_be_not_null(src, false);
6896   Node* src_start = array_element_address(src, ofs, src_elem);
6897 
6898   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
6899   const char* stub_name = NULL;
6900   address     stub_addr = NULL;
6901   bool        long_state = false;
6902 
6903   switch (predicate) {
6904   case 0:
6905     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
6906       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
6907       stub_name = "sha1_implCompressMB";
6908       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha1_implCompressMB();
6909     }
6910     break;
6911   case 1:
6912     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
6913       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
6914       stub_name = "sha256_implCompressMB";
6915       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha256_implCompressMB();
6916     }
6917     break;
6918   case 2:
6919     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
6920       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
6921       stub_name = "sha512_implCompressMB";
6922       stub_addr = StubRoutines::sha512_implCompressMB();
6923       long_state = true;
6924     }
6925     break;
6926   default:
6927     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
6928   }
6929   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
6930     assert(stub_addr != NULL, "Stub is generated");
6931     if (stub_addr == NULL) return false;
6932 
6933     // get DigestBase klass to lookup for SHA klass
6934     const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBase_obj)->isa_instptr();
6935     assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBase_obj is not instance???");
6936     assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
6937 
6938     ciKlass* klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
6939     assert(klass_SHA->is_loaded(), "predicate checks that this class is loaded");
6940     ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
6941     return inline_sha_implCompressMB(digestBase_obj, instklass_SHA, long_state, stub_addr, stub_name, src_start, ofs, limit);
6942   }
6943   return false;
6944 }
6945 //------------------------------inline_sha_implCompressMB-----------------------
6946 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_sha_implCompressMB(Node* digestBase_obj, ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA,
6947                                                bool long_state, address stubAddr, const char *stubName,
6948                                                Node* src_start, Node* ofs, Node* limit) {
6949   const TypeKlassPtr* aklass = TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA);
6950   const TypeOopPtr* xtype = aklass->as_instance_type();
6951   Node* sha_obj = new CheckCastPPNode(control(), digestBase_obj, xtype);
6952   sha_obj = _gvn.transform(sha_obj);
6953 
6954   Node* state;
6955   if (long_state) {
6956     state = get_state_from_sha5_object(sha_obj);
6957   } else {
6958     state = get_state_from_sha_object(sha_obj);
6959   }
6960   if (state == NULL) return false;
6961 
6962   // Call the stub.
6963   Node* call = make_runtime_call(RC_LEAF|RC_NO_FP,
6964                                  OptoRuntime::digestBase_implCompressMB_Type(),
6965                                  stubAddr, stubName, TypePtr::BOTTOM,
6966                                  src_start, state, ofs, limit);
6967   // return ofs (int)
6968   Node* result = _gvn.transform(new ProjNode(call, TypeFunc::Parms));
6969   set_result(result);
6970 
6971   return true;
6972 }
6973 
6974 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha_object-----------------------
6975 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha_object(Node *sha_object) {
6976   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[I", /*is_exact*/ false);
6977   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA/SHA2");
6978   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6979 
6980   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6981   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_INT);
6982   return state;
6983 }
6984 
6985 //------------------------------get_state_from_sha5_object-----------------------
6986 Node * LibraryCallKit::get_state_from_sha5_object(Node *sha_object) {
6987   Node* sha_state = load_field_from_object(sha_object, "state", "[J", /*is_exact*/ false);
6988   assert (sha_state != NULL, "wrong version of sun.security.provider.SHA5");
6989   if (sha_state == NULL) return (Node *) NULL;
6990 
6991   // now have the array, need to get the start address of the state array
6992   Node* state = array_element_address(sha_state, intcon(0), T_LONG);
6993   return state;
6994 }
6995 
6996 //----------------------------inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate----------------------------
6997 // Return node representing slow path of predicate check.
6998 // the pseudo code we want to emulate with this predicate is:
6999 //    if (digestBaseObj instanceof SHA/SHA2/SHA5) do_intrinsic, else do_javapath
7000 //
7001 Node* LibraryCallKit::inline_digestBase_implCompressMB_predicate(int predicate) {
7002   assert(UseSHA1Intrinsics || UseSHA256Intrinsics || UseSHA512Intrinsics,
7003          "need SHA1/SHA256/SHA512 instruction support");
7004   assert((uint)predicate < 3, "sanity");
7005 
7006   // The receiver was checked for NULL already.
7007   Node* digestBaseObj = argument(0);
7008 
7009   // get DigestBase klass for instanceOf check
7010   const TypeInstPtr* tinst = _gvn.type(digestBaseObj)->isa_instptr();
7011   assert(tinst != NULL, "digestBaseObj is null");
7012   assert(tinst->klass()->is_loaded(), "DigestBase is not loaded");
7013 
7014   const char* klass_SHA_name = NULL;
7015   switch (predicate) {
7016   case 0:
7017     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
7018       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA class
7019       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA";
7020     }
7021     break;
7022   case 1:
7023     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
7024       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA2 class
7025       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA2";
7026     }
7027     break;
7028   case 2:
7029     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
7030       // we want to do an instanceof comparison against the SHA5 class
7031       klass_SHA_name = "sun/security/provider/SHA5";
7032     }
7033     break;
7034   default:
7035     fatal("unknown SHA intrinsic predicate: %d", predicate);
7036   }
7037 
7038   ciKlass* klass_SHA = NULL;
7039   if (klass_SHA_name != NULL) {
7040     klass_SHA = tinst->klass()->as_instance_klass()->find_klass(ciSymbol::make(klass_SHA_name));
7041   }
7042   if ((klass_SHA == NULL) || !klass_SHA->is_loaded()) {
7043     // if none of SHA/SHA2/SHA5 is loaded, we never take the intrinsic fast path
7044     Node* ctrl = control();
7045     set_control(top()); // no intrinsic path
7046     return ctrl;
7047   }
7048   ciInstanceKlass* instklass_SHA = klass_SHA->as_instance_klass();
7049 
7050   Node* instofSHA = gen_instanceof(digestBaseObj, makecon(TypeKlassPtr::make(instklass_SHA)));
7051   Node* cmp_instof = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(instofSHA, intcon(1)));
7052   Node* bool_instof = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp_instof, BoolTest::ne));
7053   Node* instof_false = generate_guard(bool_instof, NULL, PROB_MIN);
7054 
7055   return instof_false;  // even if it is NULL
7056 }
7057 
7058 //-------------inline_fma-----------------------------------
7059 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fma(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7060   Node *a = NULL;
7061   Node *b = NULL;
7062   Node *c = NULL;
7063   Node* result = NULL;
7064   switch (id) {
7065   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaD:
7066     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 6, "fma has 3 parameters of size 2 each.");
7067     // no receiver since it is static method
7068     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7069     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7070     c = round_double_node(argument(4));
7071     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaDNode(control(), a, b, c));
7072     break;
7073   case vmIntrinsics::_fmaF:
7074     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 3, "fma has 3 parameters of size 1 each.");
7075     a = argument(0);
7076     b = argument(1);
7077     c = argument(2);
7078     result = _gvn.transform(new FmaFNode(control(), a, b, c));
7079     break;
7080   default:
7081     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7082   }
7083   set_result(result);
7084   return true;
7085 }
7086 
7087 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_character_compare(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7088   // argument(0) is receiver
7089   Node* codePoint = argument(1);
7090   Node* n = NULL;
7091 
7092   switch (id) {
7093     case vmIntrinsics::_isDigit :
7094       n = new DigitNode(control(), codePoint);
7095       break;
7096     case vmIntrinsics::_isLowerCase :
7097       n = new LowerCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7098       break;
7099     case vmIntrinsics::_isUpperCase :
7100       n = new UpperCaseNode(control(), codePoint);
7101       break;
7102     case vmIntrinsics::_isWhitespace :
7103       n = new WhitespaceNode(control(), codePoint);
7104       break;
7105     default:
7106       fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7107   }
7108 
7109   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7110   return true;
7111 }
7112 
7113 //------------------------------inline_fp_min_max------------------------------
7114 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_fp_min_max(vmIntrinsics::ID id) {
7115 /* DISABLED BECAUSE METHOD DATA ISN'T COLLECTED PER CALL-SITE, SEE JDK-8015416.
7116 
7117   // The intrinsic should be used only when the API branches aren't predictable,
7118   // the last one performing the most important comparison. The following heuristic
7119   // uses the branch statistics to eventually bail out if necessary.
7120 
7121   ciMethodData *md = callee()->method_data();
7122 
7123   if ( md != NULL && md->is_mature() && md->invocation_count() > 0 ) {
7124     ciCallProfile cp = caller()->call_profile_at_bci(bci());
7125 
7126     if ( ((double)cp.count()) / ((double)md->invocation_count()) < 0.8 ) {
7127       // Bail out if the call-site didn't contribute enough to the statistics.
7128       return false;
7129     }
7130 
7131     uint taken = 0, not_taken = 0;
7132 
7133     for (ciProfileData *p = md->first_data(); md->is_valid(p); p = md->next_data(p)) {
7134       if (p->is_BranchData()) {
7135         taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->taken();
7136         not_taken = ((ciBranchData*)p)->not_taken();
7137       }
7138     }
7139 
7140     double balance = (((double)taken) - ((double)not_taken)) / ((double)md->invocation_count());
7141     balance = balance < 0 ? -balance : balance;
7142     if ( balance > 0.2 ) {
7143       // Bail out if the most important branch is predictable enough.
7144       return false;
7145     }
7146   }
7147 */
7148 
7149   Node *a = NULL;
7150   Node *b = NULL;
7151   Node *n = NULL;
7152   switch (id) {
7153   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:
7154   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:
7155     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 2, "minF/maxF has 2 parameters of size 1 each.");
7156     a = argument(0);
7157     b = argument(1);
7158     break;
7159   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:
7160   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:
7161     assert(callee()->signature()->size() == 4, "minD/maxD has 2 parameters of size 2 each.");
7162     a = round_double_node(argument(0));
7163     b = round_double_node(argument(2));
7164     break;
7165   default:
7166     fatal_unexpected_iid(id);
7167     break;
7168   }
7169   switch (id) {
7170   case vmIntrinsics::_maxF:  n = new MaxFNode(a, b);  break;
7171   case vmIntrinsics::_minF:  n = new MinFNode(a, b);  break;
7172   case vmIntrinsics::_maxD:  n = new MaxDNode(a, b);  break;
7173   case vmIntrinsics::_minD:  n = new MinDNode(a, b);  break;
7174   default:  fatal_unexpected_iid(id);  break;
7175   }
7176   set_result(_gvn.transform(n));
7177   return true;
7178 }
7179 
7180 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_profileBoolean() {
7181   Node* counts = argument(1);
7182   const TypeAryPtr* ary = NULL;
7183   ciArray* aobj = NULL;
7184   if (counts->is_Con()
7185       && (ary = counts->bottom_type()->isa_aryptr()) != NULL
7186       && (aobj = ary->const_oop()->as_array()) != NULL
7187       && (aobj->length() == 2)) {
7188     // Profile is int[2] where [0] and [1] correspond to false and true value occurrences respectively.
7189     jint false_cnt = aobj->element_value(0).as_int();
7190     jint  true_cnt = aobj->element_value(1).as_int();
7191 
7192     if (C->log() != NULL) {
7193       C->log()->elem("observe source='profileBoolean' false='%d' true='%d'",
7194                      false_cnt, true_cnt);
7195     }
7196 
7197     if (false_cnt + true_cnt == 0) {
7198       // According to profile, never executed.
7199       uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7200                           Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7201       return true;
7202     }
7203 
7204     // result is a boolean (0 or 1) and its profile (false_cnt & true_cnt)
7205     // is a number of each value occurrences.
7206     Node* result = argument(0);
7207     if (false_cnt == 0 || true_cnt == 0) {
7208       // According to profile, one value has been never seen.
7209       int expected_val = (false_cnt == 0) ? 1 : 0;
7210 
7211       Node* cmp  = _gvn.transform(new CmpINode(result, intcon(expected_val)));
7212       Node* test = _gvn.transform(new BoolNode(cmp, BoolTest::eq));
7213 
7214       IfNode* check = create_and_map_if(control(), test, PROB_ALWAYS, COUNT_UNKNOWN);
7215       Node* fast_path = _gvn.transform(new IfTrueNode(check));
7216       Node* slow_path = _gvn.transform(new IfFalseNode(check));
7217 
7218       { // Slow path: uncommon trap for never seen value and then reexecute
7219         // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() to bump the count, so JIT knows
7220         // the value has been seen at least once.
7221         PreserveJVMState pjvms(this);
7222         PreserveReexecuteState preexecs(this);
7223         jvms()->set_should_reexecute(true);
7224 
7225         set_control(slow_path);
7226         set_i_o(i_o());
7227 
7228         uncommon_trap_exact(Deoptimization::Reason_intrinsic,
7229                             Deoptimization::Action_reinterpret);
7230       }
7231       // The guard for never seen value enables sharpening of the result and
7232       // returning a constant. It allows to eliminate branches on the same value
7233       // later on.
7234       set_control(fast_path);
7235       result = intcon(expected_val);
7236     }
7237     // Stop profiling.
7238     // MethodHandleImpl::profileBoolean() has profiling logic in its bytecode.
7239     // By replacing method body with profile data (represented as ProfileBooleanNode
7240     // on IR level) we effectively disable profiling.
7241     // It enables full speed execution once optimized code is generated.
7242     Node* profile = _gvn.transform(new ProfileBooleanNode(result, false_cnt, true_cnt));
7243     C->record_for_igvn(profile);
7244     set_result(profile);
7245     return true;
7246   } else {
7247     // Continue profiling.
7248     // Profile data isn't available at the moment. So, execute method's bytecode version.
7249     // Usually, when GWT LambdaForms are profiled it means that a stand-alone nmethod
7250     // is compiled and counters aren't available since corresponding MethodHandle
7251     // isn't a compile-time constant.
7252     return false;
7253   }
7254 }
7255 
7256 bool LibraryCallKit::inline_isCompileConstant() {
7257   Node* n = argument(0);
7258   set_result(n->is_Con() ? intcon(1) : intcon(0));
7259   return true;
7260 }
